My , how good it taste !
He go all around the tree , strip off the bark .
He stand up on his long hind leg and reach as high a he could .
Then he dig the snow away and eat down as far a he could .
When he could get no more tender young bark , he go on to the next tree .
Now though Peter do n't know it , he be in the very bad kind of mischief .
You see , when he take off all the bark all the way around the young peach tree he kill the tree , for you know it be on the inside of the bark that the sap which give life to a tree and make it grow go up from the root to all the branch .
So when Peter eat the bark all the way around the trunk of the young tree , he have make it impossible for the sap to come up in the spring .
Oh , it be the bad kind of mischief that Peter Rabbit be in .
But Peter do n't know it , and he keep right on fill that big stomach of his and enjoy it so much that he forget to watch out for danger .
Suddenly , just a he have begin on another tree , a great roar right behind him make him jump almost out of his skin .
He know that voice , and without wait to even look behind him , he start for the stone wall on the other side of the orchard .
Right at his heel , his great mouth wide open , be Bowser the Hound .
CHAPTER XIV Farmer Brown Sets a Trap Peter Rabbit be in trouble .
He have get into mischief and now , like everyone who get into mischief , he wish that he have n't .
The bad of it be that he be a long way from his home in the dear Old Briar-patch , and he do n't know how he ever could get back there again .
Where be he ?
Why , in the stone wall on one side of Farmer Brown 's young peach orchard .
How Peter bless the old stone wall in which he have find a safe hiding-place !
Bowser have hang around nearly all night , so that Peter have not dare to try to go home .
Now it be daylight , and Peter know it would not be safe to put his nose outside .
Peter be worry , so worried that he could n't go to sleep a he usually do in the daytime .
So he sit hide in the old wall and wait and watch .
By and by he saw Farmer Brown and Farmer Brown 's boy come out into the orchard .
Right away they saw the mischief which Peter have do , and he could tell by the sound of their voice that they be very , very angry .
They go away , but before long they be back again , and all day long Peter watch them work put something around each of the young peach-trees .
Peter grow so curious that he forget all about his trouble and how far away from home he be .
He could hardly wait for night to come so that he might see what they have be do .
Just a jolly , round , red Mr. Sun start to go to bed behind the Purple Hills , Farmer Brown and his boy start back to the house .
Farmer Brown be smile now .
`` I guess that will fix him ! ''
he say .
`` Now what do he mean by that ? ''
think Peter .
`` Whom will it fix ?
Can it be me ?
I do n't need any fixing . ''
He wait just as long a he could .
When all be still , and the moonlight have begin to make shadow of the tree on the snow , Peter very cautiously creep out of his hiding-place .
Bowser the Hound be nowhere in sight , and everything be a quiet and peaceful a it have be when he first come into the orchard the night before .
Peter have fully make up his mind to go straight home as fast a his long leg would take him , but his dreadful curiosity insist that first he must find out what Farmer Brown and his boy have be do to the young peach tree .
So Peter hurry over to the near tree .
All around the trunk of the tree , from the ground clear up high than Peter could reach , be wrap wire netting .
Peter could n't get so much a a nibble of the delicious bark .
He have n't intend to take any , for he have mean to go right straight home , but now that he could n't get any , he want some more than ever , -- just a bite .
Peter look around .
Everything be quiet .
He would try the next tree , and then he would go home .
But the next tree be wrap with wire .
Peter hesitate , look around , turn to go home , think of how good that bark have taste the night before , hesitate again , and then hurry over to the third tree .
It be protect just like the others .
Then Peter forget all about go home .
He want some of that delicious bark , and he run from one tree to another as fast a he could go .
-LSB- Illustration : The tree trunk be wrap in wire netting . -RSB-
At last , way down at the end of the orchard , Peter find a tree that have no wire around it .
`` They must have forget this one ! ''
he think , and his eye sparkle .
All around on the snow be a lot of little , shiny wire , but Peter do n't notice them .
All he saw be that delicious bark on the young peach tree .
He hop right into the middle of the wire , and then , just a he reach up to take the first bite of bark , he felt something tug at one of his hind leg .
CHAPTER XV Peter Rabbit Is Caught in a Snare When Peter Rabbit , reach up to nibble the bark of one of Farmer Brown 's young tree , felt something tug at one of his hind leg , he be so startled that he jump to get away .
Instead of do this , he fell flat on his face .
The thing on his hind leg have tighten and hold him fast .
A great fear come to Peter Rabbit , and lie there in the snow , he kick and struggle with all his might .
But the more he kick , the tighter grow that hateful thing on his leg !
Finally he grow too tired to kick any more and lay still .
The dreadful thing that hold him hurt his leg , but it do n't pull when he lay still .
When he have grow a little calmer , Peter sit up to examine the thing which hold him so fast .
It be something like one of the blackberry vines he have sometimes trip over , only it be bright and shiny , and have no branch or tiny pricker , and one end be fasten to a stake .
Peter try to bite off the shiny thing , but even his great , sharp front teeth could n't cut it .
Then Peter know what it be .
It be wire !
It be a snare which Farmer Brown have set to catch him , and which he have walk right into because he have be so greedy for the bark of the young peach tree that he have not use his eye to look out for danger .
Oh , how Peter Rabbit do wish that he have not be so curious to know what Farmer Brown have be do that day , and that he have go straight home a he have mean to do , instead of try to get one more meal of young peach bark !
Big tear roll down Peter 's cheek .
What should he do ?
What could he do ?
For a long time Peter sit in the moonlight , try to think of something to do .
At last he think of the stake to which that hateful wire be fasten .
The stake be of wood , and Peter 's teeth would cut wood .
Peter 's heart give a great leap of hope , and he begin at once to dig away the snow from around the stake , and then settle himself to gnaw the stake in two .
Peter have be hard at work on the stake a long time and have it a little more than half cut through , when he hear a loud sniff down at the other end of the orchard .
He look up to see -- whom do you think ?
Why , Bowser the Hound !
He have n't see Peter yet , but he have already find Peter 's track , and it would be but a few minute before he find Peter himself .
Poor Peter Rabbit !
There be n't time to finish cut off the stake .
What could he do ?
He make a frightened jump just a he have when he first felt the wire tugging at his leg .
Just a before , he be throw flat on his face .
He scramble to his foot and jump again , only to be throw just a before .
Just then Bowser the Hound saw him and open his mouth send forth a great roar .
Peter make one more frantic jump .
Snap !
the stake have break !
Peter pitch forward on his head , turn a somersault , and scramble to his foot .
He be free at last !
That be , he could run , but after him drag a piece of the stake .
How Peter do run !
It be hard work , for you know he have to drag that piece of stake after him .
But he do it , and just in time he crawl into the old stone wall on one side of the orchard , while Bowser the Hound bark his disappointment to the moon .
CHAPTER XVI Peter Rabbit 's Hard Journey Peter Rabbit sit in the old stone wall along one side of Farmer Brown 's orchard , wait for Mrs . Moon to put out her light and leave the world in darkness until jolly , round , red Mr. Sun should kick off his rosy bedclothes and begin his daily climb up in the blue , blue sky .
In the winter , Mr. Sun be a late sleeper , and Peter know that there would be two or three hour after Mrs . Moon put out her light when it would be quite dark .
And Peter also know too that by this time Hooty the Owl would probably have catch his dinner .
So would old Granny Fox and Reddy Fox .
Bowser the Hound would be too sleepy to be on the watch .
It would be the very safe time for Peter to try to get to his home in the dear Old Briar-patch .
So Peter wait and wait .
Twice Bowser the Hound , who have chase him into the old wall , come over and bark at him and try to get at him .
But the old wall keep Peter safe , and Bowser give it up .
And all the time Peter sit wait he be in great pain .
You see that shiny wire be draw so tight that it cut into his flesh and hurt dreadfully , and to the other end of the wire be fasten a piece of wood , part of the stake to which the snare have be make fast and which Peter have manage to gnaw and break off .
It be on account of this that Peter be wait for Mrs . Moon to put out her light .
He know that with that stake drag after him he would have to go very slowly , and he could not run any more risk of danger than he actually have to .
So he wait and wait , and by and by , sure enough , Mrs . Moon put out her light .
Peter wait a little long , listen with all his might .
Everything be still .
Then Peter creep out of the old stone wall .
Right away trouble begin .
The stake drag at the end of the wire fast to his leg caught among the stone and pull Peter up short .
My , how it do hurt !
It make the tear come .
But Peter shut his teeth hard , and turn back , he work until he get the stake free .
Then he start on once more , drag the stake after him .
Very slowly across the orchard and under the fence on the other side creep Peter Rabbit , his leg so stiff and sore that he could hardly touch it to the snow , and all the time drag that piece of stake , which seem to grow heavy and hard to drag every minute .
Peter do not dare to go out across the open field , for fear some danger might happen along , and he would have no place to hide .
So he creep along close to the fence where bush grow , and this make it very , very hard , for the drag stake be forever catch in the bush with a yank at the sore leg which bring Peter up short with a squeal of pain .
This be bad enough , but all the time Peter be fill with a dreadful fear that Hooty the Owl or Granny Fox might just happen along .
He have to stop to rest very , very often , and then he would listen and listen .
Over and over again he say to himself : `` Oh , dear , whatever do I go up to the young peach orchard for when I know I have no business there ?
Why could n't I have be content with all the good thing that be mine in the Green Forest and on the Green Meadows ?
Oh , dear !
Oh , dear ! ''
Just a jolly , round , red Mr. Sun begin to light up the Green Meadows , Peter Rabbit reach the dear Old Briar-patch .
Danny Meadow Mouse be sit on the edge of it anxiously watch for him .
Peter crawl up and start to creep in along one of his little private path .
He get in himself , but the drag stake caught among the bramble , and Peter just fell down in the snow right where he be , too tired and wear out to move .
CHAPTER XVII Danny Meadow Mouse Becomes Worried Danny Meadow Mouse limp around through the dear Old Briar-patch , where he have live with Peter Rabbit ever since he have squirm out of the claw of Hooty the Owl and drop there , right at the foot of Peter Rabbit .
Danny limp because he be still lame and sore from Hooty 's terrible claw , but he do n't let himself think much about that , because he be so thankful to be alive at all .
So he limp around in the Old Briar-patch , pick up seed which have fall on the snow , and sometimes pull down a few of the red berry which cling all winter to the wild rise bush .
The seed in these be very nice indeed , and Danny always felt especially good after a meal of them .
Danny Meadow Mouse have grow very fond of Peter Rabbit , for Peter have be very , very good to him .
Danny felt that he never , never could repay all of Peter 's kindness .
It have be very good of Peter to offer to share the Old Briar-patch with Danny , because Danny be so far from his own home that it would not be safe for him to try to get back there .
But Peter have do more than that .
He have take care of Danny , such good care , during the first few day after Danny 's escape from Hooty the Owl .
He have bring good thing to eat while Danny be too weak and sore to get thing for himself .
Oh , Peter have be very good indeed to him !
But now , a Danny limp around , he be not happy .
No , sir , he be not happy .
The truth be , Danny Meadow Mouse be worry .
It be a different kind of worry from any he have know before .
You see , for the first time in his life , Danny be worry about someone else .
He be worry about Peter Rabbit .
Peter have be go from the Old Briar-patch a whole night and a whole day .
He often be go all night , but never all day too .
Danny be sure that something have happen to Peter .
He think of how he have beg Peter not to go up to Farmer Brown 's young peach orchard .
He have felt in his bone that it be not safe , that something dreadful would happen to Peter .
How Peter have laugh at him and bravely start off !
Why have n't he come home ?
As he limp around , Danny talk to himself : `` Why can not people be content With all the good thing that be send , And mind their own affair at home Instead of go forth to roam ? ''
It be now the second night since Peter Rabbit have go away .
Danny Meadow Mouse could n't sleep at all .
Round and round through the Old Briar-patch he limp , and finally sit down at the edge of it to wait and watch .
At last , just a jolly , round , red Mr. Sun send his first long ray of light across the Green Meadows , Danny saw something crawling towards the Old Briar-patch .
He rub his eye and look again .
It be -- no , it could n't be -- yes , it be Peter Rabbit !
But what be the matter with him ?
Always before Peter have come home lipperty-lipperty-lipperty-lip , but now he be crawl , actually crawl !
Danny Meadow Mouse do n't know what to make of it .
Nearer and nearer come Peter .
Something be follow him .
No , Peter be drag something after him .
At last Peter start to crawl along one of his little private path into the Old Briar-patch .
The thing drag behind caught in the bramble , and Peter fell headlong in the snow , too tired and wear out to move .
Then Danny saw what the trouble be .
A wire be fast to one of Peter 's long hind leg , and to the other end of the wire be fasten part of a stake .
Peter have be catch in a snare !
Danny hurry over to Peter and tear stand in his eye .
`` Poor Peter Rabbit !
Oh , I 'm so sorry , Peter ! ''
he whisper .
CHAPTER XVIII Danny Meadow Mouse Returns a Kindness There Peter Rabbit lay .
He have drag that piece of stake a long way , a very long way , indeed .
But now he could drag it no farther , for it have catch in the bramble bush .
So Peter just drop on the snow and cry .
Yes , sir , he cry !
You see he be so tired and wear out and frightened , and his leg be so stiff and sore and hurt him so !
And then it be so dreadful to actually get home and be stop right on your very own doorstep .
So Peter just lay there and cry .
Just suppose old Granny Fox should come poke around and find Peter catch that way !
All she would have to do would be to get hold of that hateful stake caught in the bramble bush and pull Peter out where she could get him .
Do you wonder that Peter cry ?
By and by he become aware that someone be wipe away his tear .
It be Danny Meadow Mouse .
And Danny be sing in a funny little voice .
Pretty soon Peter stop cry and listen , and this be what he hear : `` Is n't any use to cry !
Not a bit !
Not a bit !
Wipe your eye and wipe 'em dry !
Use your wit !
Use your wit !
Just remember that to-morrow Never bring a single sorrow .
Yesterday have go forever And to-morrow get here never .
Chase your worry all away ; Nothing 's bad than just to-day . ''
Peter smile in spite of himself .
`` That 's right !
That 's right !
Smile away , Peter Rabbit .
Smile away !
Your trouble , sir , be all to-day .
And between you and me , I do n't believe they be so bad a you think they be .
Now you lie still just where you be , while I go see what can be do . ''
With that off whisk Danny Meadow Mouse as spry a you please , in spite of his lame leg , and in a few minute Peter know by little twitch of the wire on his leg that Danny be do something at the other end .
He be .
Danny Meadow Mouse have set out to gnaw that piece of stake all to splinter .
So there he sit and gnaw and gnaw and gnaw .
Jolly , round , red Mr. Sun climb high and higher in the sky , and Danny Meadow Mouse grow hungry , but still he keep right on gnaw at that bothersome stake .

By and by , happen to look across the snow-covered Green Meadows , he saw something that make his heart jump .
It be Farmer Brown 's boy come straight over towards the dear Old Briar-patch .
Danny do n't say a word to Peter Rabbit , but gnaw faster than ever .
Farmer Brown 's boy be almost there when Danny stop gnaw .
There be only a tiny bit of the stake leave now , and Danny hurry to tell Peter Rabbit that there be nothing to stop him now from go to his most secret retreat in the very heart of the Old Briar-patch .
While Peter slowly drag his way along , Danny trot behind to see that the wire do not catch on the bush .
They have safely reach Peter Rabbit 's secret retreat when Farmer Brown 's boy come up to the edge of the dear Old Briar-patch .
`` So this be where that rabbit that kill our peach tree live ! ''
say he .
`` We 'll try a few snare and put you out of mischief . ''
And for the rest of the afternoon Farmer Brown 's boy be very busy around the edge of the Old Briar-patch .
CHAPTER XIX Peter Rabbit and Danny Meadow Mouse Live High Peter Rabbit sit in his secret place in the dear Old Briar-patch with one of his long hind leg all swell up and terribly sore because of the fine wire fast around it and cut into it .
He could hear Farmer Brown 's boy go around on the edge of the dear Old Briar-patch and stop every little while to do something .
In spite of his pain , Peter be curious .
Finally he call Danny Meadow Mouse .
`` Danny , you be small and can keep out of sight easy than I can .
Go as near a ever you dare to Farmer Brown 's boy and find out what he be do , '' say Peter Rabbit .
So Danny Meadow Mouse creep out a near to Farmer Brown 's boy a ever he dare and study and study to make out what Farmer Brown 's boy be do .
By and by he return to Peter Rabbit .
`` I do n't know what he 's do , Peter , but he 's put something in every one of your private little paths lead into the Briar-patch from the Green Meadows . ''
`` Ha ! ''
say Peter Rabbit .
`` There be little loop of that queer stuff you 've get hang to your leg , Peter , '' continue Danny Meadow Mouse .
`` Just so ! ''
say Peter Rabbit .
`` And he 's put cabbage leaf and piece of apple all around , '' say Danny .
`` We must be careful ! ''
say Peter Rabbit .
Peter 's leg be in a very bad way , indeed , and Peter suffer a great deal of pain .
The bad of it be , he do n't know how to get off the wire that be cut into it so .
He have try to cut the wire with his big teeth , but he could n't do it .
Danny Meadow Mouse have try and try to gnaw the wire , but it be n't the least bit of use .
But Danny be n't easily discourage , and he keep work and work at it .
Once he think he felt it slip a little .
He say nothing , but keep right on work .
Pretty soon he be sure that it slip .
He go right on work harder than ever .
By and by he have it so loose that he slip it right off of Peter 's leg , and Peter do n't know anything about it .
You see , that cruel wire snare have be so tight that Peter do n't have any feeling except of pain leave in his leg , and so when Danny Meadow Mouse pull the cruel wire snare off , Peter do n't know it until Danny hold it up in front of him .
My , how thankful Peter be , and how he do thank Danny Meadow Mouse !
But Danny say that it be nothing at all , just nothing at all , and that he owe more than that to Peter Rabbit for be so good to him and let him live in the dear Old Briar-patch .
It be a long time before Peter could hop a he use to , but after the first day he manage to get around .
He find that Farmer Brown 's boy have spread those miserable wire snare in every one of his private little path .
But Peter know what they be now .
He show Danny Meadow Mouse how he , because he be so small , could safely run about among the snare and steal all the cabbage leave and apple which Farmer Brown 's boy have put there for bait .
Danny Meadow Mouse think this great fun and a great joke on Farmer Brown 's boy .
So every day he steal the bait , and he and Peter Rabbit live high while Peter 's leg be get well .
And all the time Farmer Brown 's boy wonder why he could n't catch Peter Rabbit .
CHAPTER XX Timid Danny Meadow Mouse Danny Meadow Mouse be timid .
Everybody say so , and what everybody say ought to be so .
But just a anybody can make a mistake sometimes , so can everybody .
Still , in this case , it be quite likely that everybody be right .
Danny Meadow Mouse be timid .
Ask Peter Rabbit .
Ask Sammy Jay .
Ask Striped Chipmunk .
They will all tell you the same thing .
Sammy Jay might even tell you that Danny be afraid of his own shadow , or that he try to run away from his own tail .
Of course this be n't true .
Sammy Jay like to say mean thing .
It be n't fair to Danny Meadow Mouse to believe what Sammy Jay say .
But the fact be Danny certainly be timid .
More than this , he be n't ashamed of it -- not the least little bit .
`` You see , it 's this way , '' say Danny , a he sit on his doorstep one sunny morning talk to his friend , old Mr. Toad .
`` If I be n't afraid , I would n't be all the time watch out , and if I be n't all the time watch out , I would n't have any more chance than that foolish red ant run across in front of you . ''
Old Mr. Toad look where Danny be point , and his tongue dart out and back again so quickly that Danny be n't sure that he saw it at all , but when he look for the ant it be nowhere to be see , and there be a satisfied twinkle in Mr. Toad 's eye .
There be an answer twinkle in Danny 's own eye a he continue .
`` No , sir , '' say he , `` I would n't stand a particle more chance than that foolish ant do .
Now if I be big and strong , like Old Man Coyote , or have swift wing , like Skimmer the Swallow , or be so homely and ugly-looking that no one want me , like -- like -- '' Danny hesitate and then finish rather lamely , `` like some folk I know , I suppose I would n't be afraid . ''
Old Mr. Toad look up sharply when Danny mention homely and ugly-looking people , but Danny be gaze far out across the Green Meadows and look so innocent that Mr. Toad conclude that he could n't have have him in mind .
`` Well , '' say he , thoughtfully scratch his nose , `` I suppose you may be right , but for my part fear seem a very foolish thing .
Now , I do n't know what it be .
I mind my own business , and no one ever bother me .
I should think it would be a very uncomfortable feeling . ''
`` It be , '' reply Danny , `` but , a I say before , it be a very good thing to keep one on guard when there be a many watch for one a there be for me .
Now there 's Mr. Blacksnake and -- '' `` Where ? ''
exclaim old Mr. Toad , turn as pale a a toad can turn , and look uneasily and anxiously in every direction .
Danny turn his head to hide a smile .
If old Mr. Toad be n't show fear , no one ever do .
`` Oh , '' say he , `` I do n't mean that he be anywhere around here now .
What I be go to say be that there be Mr. Blacksnake and Granny Fox and Reddy Fox and Redtail the Hawk and Hooty the Owl and others I might name , always watch for a chance to make a dinner from poor little me .
Do you wonder that I be afraid most of the time ? ''
`` No , '' reply old Mr. Toad .
`` No , I do n't wonder that you be afraid .
It must be dreadful to feel hungry eye be watch for you every minute of the day and night , too . ''
`` Oh , it 's not so bad , '' reply Danny .
`` It 's rather exciting .
Besides , it keep my wit sharp all the time .
I be afraid I should find life very dull indeed if , like you , I fear nothing and nobody .
By the way , see how queerly that grass be move over there .
It look a if Mr. Blacksnake -- Why , Mr. Toad , where be you go in such a hurry ? ''
`` I 've just remember an important engagement with my cousin , Grandfather Frog , at the Smiling Pool , '' shout old Mr. Toad over his shoulder , a he hurry so that he fell over his own foot .
Danny chuckle a he sit alone on his doorstep .
`` Oh , no , old Mr. Toad do n't know what fear be ! ''
say he .
`` Funny how some people wo n't admit what everybody can see for themselves .
Now , I be afraid , and I 'm willing to say so . ''
CHAPTER XXI An Exciting Day for Danny Meadow Mouse Danny Meadow Mouse start along one of his private little paths very early one morning .
He be on his way to get a supply of a certain kind of grass seed of which he be very fond .
He have be think about that seed for some time and wait for it to get ripe .
Now it be just right , a he have find out the day before by a visit to the place where this particular grass grow .
The only trouble be it grow a long way from Danny 's home , and to reach it he have to cross an open place where the grass be so short that he could n't make a path under it .
`` I feel it in my bone that this be go to be an exciting day , '' say Danny to himself a he trot along .
`` I suppose that if I be really wise , I would stay nearer home and do without that nice seed .
But nothing be really worth have unless it be worth work for , and that seed will taste all the good if I have hard work get it . ''
So he trot along his private little path , his ear wide open , and his eye wide open , and his little nose carefully test every Merry Little Breeze who happen along for any scent of danger which it might carry .
Most of all he depend upon his ear , for the grass be so tall that he could n't see over it , even when he sit up .
He have go only a little way when he think he hear a queer rustle behind him .
He stop to listen .
There it be again , and it certainly be right in the path behind him !
He do n't need to be tell who be make it .
There be only one who could make such a sound a that -- Mr. Blacksnake .
Now Danny can run very fast along his private little path , but he know that Mr. Blacksnake could run faster .
`` If my leg ca n't save me , my wit must , '' think Danny a he start to run as fast a ever he could .
`` I must reach that fall old hollow fence-post . ''
He be almost out of breath when he reach the post and scurry into the open end .
He know by the sound of the rustling that Mr. Blacksnake be right at his heel .
Now the old post be hollow it whole length , but halfway there be an old knot-hole just big enough for Danny to squeeze through .
Mr. Blacksnake do n't know anything about that hole ; and because it be dark inside the old post , he do n't see Danny pop through it .
Danny run back along the top of the log and be just in time to see the tip of Mr. Blacksnake 's tail disappear inside .
Then what do you think Danny do ?
Why , he follow Mr. Blacksnake right into the old post , but in do it he do n't make the least little bit of noise .
Mr. Blacksnake keep right on through the old post and out the other end , for he be sure that that be the way Danny have go .
He keep right on along the little path .
Now Danny know that he would n't go very far before he find out that he have be fool , and of course he would come back .
So Danny wait only long enough to get his breath and then run back along the path to where another little path branch off .
For just a minute he pause .
`` If Mr. Blacksnake follow me , he will be sure to think that of course I have take this other little path , '' think Danny , `` so I wo n't do it . ''
Then he run hard than ever , until he come to a place where two little path branch off , one to the right and one to the left .
He take the latter and scamper on , sure that by this time Mr. Blacksnake would be so badly fool that he would give up the chase .
And Danny be right .
`` Brains be well far than speed As wise men long ago agree , '' say Danny , a he trot on his way for the grass seed he like so well .
`` I felt it in my bone that this would be an exciting day .
I wonder what next . ''
CHAPTER XXII What Happened Next to Danny Meadow Mouse Danny be so used to narrow escape that he do n't waste any time think about them .
He do n't this time .
`` He who try to look two way at once be pretty sure to see nothing , '' say Danny , and he know that if he think too much about the thing that have already happen , he could n't keep a sharp watch for the thing that might happen .
Nothing more happened a he hurry along his private little path to the edge of a great patch of grass so short that he could n't hide under it .
He have to cross this , and all the way he would be in plain sight of anyone who happen to be near .
Very cautiously he peep out and look this way and look that way , not forget to look up in the sky .
He could see no one anywhere .
Drawing a long breath , Danny start across the open place as fast a his short leg could take him .
Now all the time , Redtail the Hawk have be sit in a tree some distance away , sit so still that he look like a part of the tree itself .
That be why Danny have n't see him .
But Redtail saw Danny the instant he start across the open place , for Redtail 's eye be very keen , and he can see a great distance .
With a satisfied chuckle , he spread his broad wing and start after Danny .
Just about halfway to the safety of the long grass on the other side , Danny give a hurried look behind him , and his heart seem to jump right into his mouth , for there be Redtail with his cruel claw already set to seize him !
Danny give a frightened squeak , for he think that surely this time he would be catch .
But he do n't mean to give up without try to escape .
Three jump ahead of him be a queer-looking thing .

I BILLY MINK FINDS LITTLE JOE OTTER Billy Mink run around the edge of the Smiling Pool and turn down by the Laughing Brook .

IV THE PATIENCE OF LONGLEGS THE BLUE HERON Patience often win the day When over-haste have lose the way .

Dear me !

VII GRANDFATHER FROG 'S BIG MOUTH GETS HIM IN TROUBLE Grandfather Frog have a great big mouth .
You know that .
Everybody do .
His friend of the Smiling Pool , the Laughing Brook , and the Green Meadows have tease Grandfather Frog a great deal about the size of his mouth , but he have n't mind in the least , not the very least .
You see , he learn a long time ago that a big mouth be very handy for catch foolish green fly , especially when two happen to come along together .
So he be rather proud of his big mouth , just a he be of his goggly eye .
But once in a while his big mouth get him into trouble .
It 's a way big mouth have .
It hold so much that it make him greedy sometimes .
He stuff it full after his stomach already have all that it can hold , and then of course he ca n't swallow .
Then Grandfather Frog look very foolish and silly and undignified , and everybody call him a greedy fellow who be old enough to know good and who ought to be ashamed of himself .
Perhaps he be , but he never say so , and he be almost sure to do the same thing over again the first chance he have .
Now it happen that one morning when Grandfather Frog have have a very good breakfast of foolish green fly and really do n't need another single thing to eat , who should come along but Little Joe Otter , who have be down to the Big River fishing .
He have eat all he could hold , and he be take the rest of his catch to a secret hiding-place up the Laughing Brook .
Now Grandfather Frog be very fond of fish for a change , and when he saw those that Little Joe Otter have , his eye glisten , and in spite of his full stomach his mouth water .
`` Good morning , Grandfather Frog !
Have you have your breakfast yet ? ''
call Little Joe Otter .
Grandfather Frog want to say no , but he always tell the truth .
`` Ye-e-s , '' he reply .
`` I 've have my breakfast , such a it be .
Why do you ask ? ''
`` Oh , for no reason in particular .
I just think that if you have n't , you might like a fish .
But as long a you have breakfast , of course you do n't want one , '' say Little Joe , his bright eye begin to twinkle .
He hold the fish out so that Grandfather Frog could see just how plump and nice they be .
`` Chugarum ! ''
exclaim Grandfather Frog .
`` Those certainly be very nice fish , very nice fish indeed .
It be very nice of you to think of a poor old fellow like me , and I -- er -- well , I might find room for just a little teeny , weeny one , if you can spare it . ''
Little Joe Otter know all about Grandfather Frog 's greediness .
He look at Grandfather Frog 's white and yellow waistcoat and saw how it be already stuff full to burst .
The twinkle in his eye grow more mischievous than ever a he say : `` Of course I can .
But I would n't think of give such an old friend a teeny , weeny one . ''
With that , Little Joe pick out the big fish he have and toss it over to Grandfather Frog .
It land close by his nose with a great splash , and it be almost half as big a Grandfather Frog himself .
It be plump and look so tempting that Grandfather Frog forget all about his full stomach .
He even forget to be polite and thank Little Joe Otter .
He just open his great mouth and seize the fish .
Yes , Sir , that be just what he do .
Almost before you could wink an eye , the fish have start down Grandfather Frog 's throat head first .
Now you know Grandfather Frog have no teeth , and so he can not bite thing in two .
He have to swallow them whole .
That be just what he start to do with the fish .
It go all right until the head reach his stomach .
But you ca n't put anything more into a thing already full , and Grandfather Frog 's stomach be pack as full a it could be of foolish green fly .
There the fish stuck , and gulp and swallow as hard a he could , Grandfather Frog could n't make that fish go a bit far .
Then he try to get it out again , but it have go so far down his throat that he could n't get it back .
Grandfather Frog begin to choke .
VIII SPOTTY THE TURTLE PLAYS DOCTOR Greed 's a dreadful thing to see , As everybody will agree .
At first Little Joe Otter , sit on the bank of the Smiling Pool , laugh himself almost sick a he watch Grandfather Frog try to swallow a fish almost as big a himself , when his white and yellow waistcoat be already stuff so full of foolish green fly that there be n't room for anything more .
Such greed would have be disgust , if it have n't be so very , very funny .
At least , it be funny at first , for the fish have stick , with the tail hang out of Grandfather Frog 's big mouth .
Grandfather Frog hitch this way and hitch that way on his big green lily-pad , try his best to swallow .
Twice he tumble off with a splash into the Smiling Pool .
Each time he scramble back again and roll his great goggly eye in silent appeal to Little Joe Otter to come to his aid .

-RSB- But Little Joe be laugh so that he have to hold his side , and he do n't understand that Grandfather Frog really be in trouble .

Splash !

Thank you ! ''
gasp Grandfather Frog , a he feebly crawl back on the lily-pad .

IX OLD MR. TOAD VISITS GRANDFATHER FROG Grandfather Frog and old Mr. Toad be cousin .
Of course you know that without be tell .
Everybody do .
But not everybody know that they be bear in the same place .
They be .
Yes , Sir , they be .
They be bear in the Smiling Pool .
Both have long tail and for a while no leg , and they play and swim together without ever go on shore .
In fact , when they be baby , they could n't live out of the water .
And people who saw them do n't know the difference between them and call them by the same name -- tadpole or pollywog .
But when they grow old enough to have leg and get along without tail , they part company .
You see , it be this way : Grandfather Frog -LRB- of course he be n't grandfather then -RRB- love the Smiling Pool so well that he could n't think of leave it .
He hear all about the Great World and what a wonderful place it be , but he could n't and would n't believe that there could be any nice place than the Smiling Pool , and so he make up his mind that he would live there always .
But Mr. Toad could hardly wait to get rid of his tail before turn his back on the Smiling Pool and start out to see the Great World .
Nothing that Grandfather Frog could say would stop him , and away Mr. Toad go , when he be so small that he could hide under a clover leaf .
Grandfather Frog do n't expect ever to see him again .
But he do , though it be n't for a long , long time .
And when he do come back , he have grow so that Grandfather Frog hardly know him at first .
And right then and there begin a dispute which they have keep up ever since : whether it be best to go out into the Great World or remain in the home of childhood .
Each be sure that what he have do be best , and each be sure of it to this day .
So whenever old Mr. Toad visit Grandfather Frog , a he do every once in a while , they be sure to argue and argue on this same old subject .
It be so on the day that Grandfather Frog have so nearly choke to death .
Old Mr. Toad have hear about it from one of the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind and right away have start for the Smiling Pool to pay his respect to Grandfather Frog , and to tell him how glad he be that Spotty the Turtle have come along just in time to pull the fish out of Grandfather Frog 's throat .
Now all day long Grandfather Frog have have to listen to unpleasant remark about his greediness .
It be such a splendid chance to tease him that everybody around the Smiling Pool take advantage of it .
Grandfather Frog take it good-naturedly at first , but after a while it make him cross , and by the time his cousin , old Mr. Toad , arrive , he be sulky and just grunt when Mr. Toad tell him how glad he be to find Grandfather Frog quite recover .
Old Mr. Toad pretend not to notice how out of sort Grandfather Frog be but keep right on talk .
`` If you have be out in the Great World as much a I have be , you would have know that Little Joe Otter be n't give you that fish for nothing , '' say he .
Grandfather Frog swell right out with anger .
`` Chugarum ! ''
he exclaim in his deepest , gruff voice .
`` Chugarum !
Go back to your Great World and learn to mind your own affair , Mr. Toad . ''
Right away old Mr. Toad begin to swell with anger too .

When he do find it , he say some very unpleasant thing , and right away they begin to dispute .

ask old Mr. Toad .

You 've be out in the Great World ever since you could hop , and what good have it do you ?
Tell me that !
You have n't even a decent suit of clothes to your back . ''
Grandfather Frog pat his white and yellow waistcoat a he speak and look admiringly at the reflection of his handsome green coat in the Smiling Pool .

`` People who do honest work for their living have no time to sit about in fine clothes admire themselves , '' he reply sharply .
`` I 've learn this much out in the Great World , that lazy people come to no good end , and I know enough not to choke myself to death . ''

Old Mr. Toad do n't look troubled the least bit .

X GRANDFATHER FROG STARTS OUT TO SEE THE GREAT WORLD Grandfather Frog look very solemn a he sit on his big green lily-pad in the Smiling Pool .

Now Grandfather Frog be afraid of Farmer Brown 's boy , so when he appear , Grandfather Frog stop argue with old Mr. Toad and with a great splash dive into the Smiling Pool and hide under a lily-pad .
There he stay and watch his cousin , old Mr. Toad , grin in the most provoking way , for he be n't afraid of Farmer Brown 's boy .
In fact , he have boast that they be friend .
Grandfather Frog have think that this be just an idle boast , but when he saw Farmer Brown 's boy tickle old Mr. Toad under his chin with a straw , while Mr. Toad sit perfectly still and seem to enjoy it , he know that it be true .
Grandfather Frog have not come out of his hiding-place until after old Mr. Toad have go back across the Green Meadows and Farmer Brown 's boy have go home for his supper .

He be think , think very hard .
And now , this bright , sunshiny morning , he be still think .
The fact be Grandfather Frog be begin to wonder if perhaps , after all , Mr. Toad be right .
If the Great World have teach him how to make friend with Farmer Brown 's boy , there really must be some thing worth learn there .

But right down in his heart he be begin to think that perhaps there be some thing which he could n't learn in the Smiling Pool .

`` Chugarum ! ''

`` You just mind your own affair , Jerry Muskrat , '' he retort sharply .

XI GRANDFATHER FROG IS STUBBORN `` Fee , fi , fe , fum !

XII GRANDFATHER FROG KEEPS ON Grandfather Frog be old and wise , But even age be foolish .

XIII DANNY MEADOW MOUSE FEELS RESPONSIBLE Responsible be a great big word .

XIV GRANDFATHER FROG HAS A STRANGE RIDE A thousand thing may happen to , Ten thousand thing befall , The traveler who careless be , Or think he know it all .
Grandfather Frog , jump along behind Danny Meadow Mouse up the Lone Little Path , be begin to think that Danny be the most timid and easy frighten of all the little meadow people of his acquaintance .

When he be safely across , he would wait for Grandfather Frog .
If a shadow pass over the grass , Danny would duck under the near leaf and hold his breath .
`` Foolish ! ''
mutter Grandfather Frog .
`` Foolish , foolish to be so afraid !
Now , I 'm not afraid until I see something to be afraid of .
Time enough then .
What 's the good of look for trouble all the time ?
Now , here I be out in the Great World , and I 'm not afraid .
And here 's Danny Meadow Mouse , who have live here all his life , act a if he expect something dreadful to happen any minute .
Pooh !
How very , very foolish ! ''
Now Grandfather Frog be old and in the Smiling Pool he be accounted very , very wise .
But the wise sometimes become foolish when they think that they know all there be to know .
It be so with Grandfather Frog .
It be he who be foolish and not Danny Meadow Mouse .
You see Danny know all the danger on the Green Meadows , and how many sharp eye be all the time watch for him .
He have long ago learn that the only way to feel safe be to feel afraid .
You see , then he be watch for danger every minute , and so he be n't likely to be surprise by his hungry enemy .
So while Grandfather Frog be look down on Danny for be so timid , Danny be really do the wise thing .
More than that , he be really very , very brave .
He be show Grandfather Frog the way up the Lone Little Path to see the Great World , when he himself would never , never have think of travel anywhere but along his own secret little path , just because Grandfather Frog could n't jump anywhere except where the way be fairly clear , a in the Lone Little Path , and Danny be afraid that unless Grandfather Frog have some one with him to watch out for him , he would surely come to a sad end .
The farther they go with nothing happening , the more foolish Danny 's timid way of run and hide seem to Grandfather Frog , and he be just about to tell Danny just what he think , when Danny dive into the long grass and warn Grandfather Frog to do the same .
But Grandfather Frog do n't .
`` Chugarum ! ''
say he , `` I do n't see anything to be afraid of , and I 'm not go to hide until I do . ''
So he sit still right where he be , in the middle of the Lone Little Path , look this way and that way , and see nothing to be afraid of .
And just then around a turn in the Lone Little Path come -- who do you think ?
Why Farmer Brown 's boy !
He saw Grandfather Frog and with a whoop of joy he spring for him .
Grandfather Frog give a frightened croak and jump , but he be too late .
Before he could jump again Farmer Brown 's boy have him by his long hind-legs .
`` Ha , ha ! ''
shout Farmer Brown 's boy , `` I believe this be the very old chap I have try so often to catch in the Smiling Pool .
These leg of yours will be mighty fine eating , Mr. Frog .
They will , indeed . ''
With that he tie Grandfather Frog 's leg together and go on his way across the Green Meadows with poor old Grandfather Frog dangle from the end of a string .
It be a strange ride and a most uncomfortable one , and with all his might Grandfather Frog wish he have never think of go out into the Great World .
XV GRANDFATHER FROG GIVES UP HOPE With his leg tie together , hang head down from the end of a string , Grandfather Frog be be carry he know not where by Farmer Brown 's boy .
It be dreadful .
Half-way across the Green Meadows the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind come dance along .
At first they do n't see Grandfather Frog , but presently one of them , rush up to tease Farmer Brown 's boy by blow off his hat , catch sight of Grandfather Frog .
Now the Merry Little Breezes be great friend of Grandfather Frog .
Many , many time they have blow foolish green fly over to him a he sit on his big green lily-pad , and they be very fond of him .
So when this one caught sight of him in such a dreadful position , he forget all about tease Farmer Brown 's boy .
He race away to tell the other Merry Little Breezes .
For a minute they be perfectly still .
They forget all about be merry .
`` It 's awful , just perfectly awful ! ''
cried one .
`` We must do something to help Grandfather Frog ! ''
cry another .
`` Of course we must , '' say a third .
`` But what can we do ? ''
ask a fourth .
Nobody reply .
They just think and think and think .
Finally the first one spoke .
`` We might try to comfort him a little , '' say he .
`` Of course we will do that ! ''
they shout all together .
`` And if we throw dust in the face of Farmer Brown 's boy and steal his hat , perhaps he will put Grandfather Frog down , '' continue the Merry Little Breeze .
`` The very thing ! ''
the others cry , dance about with excitement .
`` Then we can rush about and tell all Grandfather Frog 's friend what have happen to him and where he be .
Perhaps some of them can help u , '' the Little Breeze continue .
They waste no more time talk , but race after Farmer Brown 's boy as fast a they could go .
One of them , who be fast than the others , run ahead and whisper in Grandfather Frog 's ear that they be come to help him .
But poor old Grandfather Frog could n't be comfort .
He could n't see what there be that the Merry Little Breezes could do .
His leg smart where the string cut into the skin , and his head ache , for you know he be hang head down .
No , Sir , Grandfather Frog could n't be comfort .
He be in a terrible fix , and he could n't see any way out of it .
He have n't the least bit of hope left .
And all the time Farmer Brown 's boy be trudge along , whistle merrily .
You see , it do n't occur to him to think how Grandfather Frog must be suffer and how terribly frighten he must be .
He be n't cruel .
No , indeed , Farmer Brown 's boy be n't cruel .
That be , he do n't mean to be cruel .
He be just thoughtless , like a great many other boy , and girl too .
So he go whistle on his way until he reach the Long Lane lead from the Green Meadows up to Farmer Brown 's dooryard .
No sooner be he in the Long Lane than something happen .
A great cloud of dust and leaf and tiny stick be dash in his face and nearly choke him .
Dirt get in his eye .
His hat be snatch from his head and go sail over into the garden .
He drop Grandfather Frog and felt for his handkerchief to wipe the dirt from his eye .
`` Phew ! ''
exclaim Farmer Brown 's boy , a he start after his hat .
`` It 's funny where that wind come from so suddenly ! ''
But you know and I know that it be the Merry Little Breezes work together who make up that sudden wind .
And Grandfather Frog ought to have know it too , but he do n't .
You see the dust have get in his nose and eye just a it have in those of Farmer Brown 's boy , and he be so frightened and confuse that he could n't think .
So he lay just where Farmer Brown 's boy drop him , and he do n't have any more hope than before .
XVI THE MERRY LITTLE BREEZES WORK HARD The Merry Little Breezes almost shout aloud with delight when they saw Farmer Brown 's boy drop Grandfather Frog to feel for his handkerchief and wipe out the dust which they have throw in his eye .
Then he have to climb the fence and chase his hat through the garden .
They would let him almost get his hand on it and then , just a he think that he surely have it , they would snatch it away .
It be great fun for the Merry Little Breezes .
But they be not do it for fun .
No , indeed , they be not do it for fun !
They be do it to lead Farmer Brown 's boy away from Grandfather Frog .
Just as soon a they dare , they drop the hat and then separate and rush away in all direction across the Green Meadows , over to the Green Forest , and down to the Smiling Pool .
What be they go for ?
Why , to hunt for some of Grandfather Frog 's friend and ask their help .
You see , the Merry Little Breezes could make Farmer Brown 's boy drop Grandfather Frog , but they could n't untie a knot or cut a string , and this be just what have get to be do to set Grandfather Frog free , for his hind-legs be tie together .
So now they be look for some one with sharp teeth , who think enough of Grandfather Frog to come and help him .
One thought of Striped Chipmunk and start for the old stone wall to look for him .
Another go in search of Danny Meadow Mouse .
A third head for the dear Old Briar-patch after Peter Rabbit .
A fourth remembered Jimmy Skunk and how he have once set Blacky the Crow free from a snare .
A fifth remember what sharp teeth Happy Jack Squirrel have and hurry over to the Green Forest to look for him .
A sixth started straight for the Smiling Pool to tell Jerry Muskrat .
And every one of them race as fast a he could .
All this time Grandfather Frog be without hope .
Yes , Sir , poor old Grandfather Frog be wholly in despair .
You see , he do n't know what the Merry Little Breezes be try to do , and he be so frightened and confuse that he could n't think .
When Farmer Brown 's boy drop him , he lay right where he fell for a few minute .
Then , right close at hand , he saw an old board .
Without really think , he try to get to it , for there look a if there might be room for him to hide under it .
It be hard work , for you know his long hind-legs , which he use for jumping , be tie together .
The best he could do be to crawl and wriggle and pull himself along .
Just a Farmer Brown 's boy start to climb the fence back into the Long Lane , his hat in his hand , Grandfather Frog reach the old board and crawl under it .
Now when the Merry Little Breezes have throw the dust in Farmer Brown 's boy 's face and snatch his hat , he have drop Grandfather Frog in such a hurry that he do n't notice just where he do drop him , so now he do n't know the exact place to look for him .
But he know pretty near , and he have n't the least doubt but that he would find him .
He have just start to look when the dinner horn sound .
Farmer Brown 's boy hesitate .
He be hungry .
If he be late , he might lose his dinner .
He could come back later to look for Grandfather Frog , for with his leg tie Grandfather Frog could n't get far .
So , with a last look to make sure of the place , Farmer Brown 's boy start for the house .
If the Merry Little Breezes have know this , they would have felt ever so much good .
But they do n't .
So they hurry as fast a ever they could to find Grandfather Frog 's friend and work until they be almost too tired to move , for it seem a if every single one of Grandfather Frog 's friend have take that particular day to go away from home .
So while Farmer Brown 's boy eat his dinner , and Grandfather Frog lay hide under the old board in the Long Lane , the Merry Little Breezes do their best to find help for him .
XVII STRIPED CHIPMUNK CUTS THE STRING `` Hippy hop !
Flippy flop !
All on a summer day My mother turn me from the house and send me out to play ! ''
Striped Chipmunk know perfectly well that that be just nonsense , but Striped Chipmunk learn a long time ago that when you be just bubble right over with good feeling , there be fun in say and do foolish thing , and that be just how he be feel .
So he run along the old rail fence on one side of the Long Lane , say foolish thing and cut up foolish caper just because he felt so good , and all the time see all that those bright little eye of his could take in .
Now Striped Chipmunk and the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind be great friend , very great friend , indeed .
Almost every morning they have a grand frolic together .
But this morning the Merry Little Breezes have n't come over to the old stone wall where Striped Chipmunk make his home .
Anyway , they have n't come at the usual time .
Striped Chipmunk have wait a little while and then , because he be feel so good , he have decide to take a run down the Long Lane to see if anything new have happen there .
That be how it happen that when one of the Merry Little Breezes do go to look for him , and be terribly anxious to ask him to come to the help of Grandfather Frog , he be nowhere to be find .
But Striped Chipmunk do n't know anything about that .
He scamper along the top rail of the old fence , jump up on top of a post , and sit up to wash his face and hand , for Striped Chipmunk be very neat and can not bear to be the least bit dirty .
He look up and wink at Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , sail round and round way , way up in the blue , blue sky .
He chase his own tail round and round until he nearly fell off of the post .
He make a wry face in the direction of Redtail the Hawk , whom he could see sit in the top of a tall tree way over on the Green Meadows .
He scold Bowser the Hound , who happen to come trot up the Long Lane , and do n't stop scold until Bowser be out of sight .
Then he kick up his heel and whisk along the old fence again .
Half-way across a shaky old rail , he suddenly stop .
His bright eye have see something that fill him with curiosity , quite a much curiosity a Peter Rabbit would have have .
It be a piece of string .
Yes , Sir , it be a piece of string .
Now Striped Chipmunk often have find piece of string , so there be nothing particularly interesting in the string itself .
What do interest him and make him very curious be the fact that this piece of string kept moving .
Every few second it give a little jerk .
Whoever heard of a piece of string move all by itself ?
Certainly Striped Chipmunk never have .
He could n't understand it .
For a few minute he watch it from the top rail of the old fence .
Then he scurry down to the ground and , a few step at a time , stop to watch sharply between each little run , he draw nearer and near to that queer act string .
It give him a funny feel inside to see a string acting like that , so he be very careful not to get too near .
He look at it from one side , then run around and look at it from the other side .
At last he get where he could see that one end of the string be under an old board , and then he begin to understand .
Of course there be somebody hide under that old board and jerk the string .

-RSB- Striped Chipmunk sit down and scratch his head thoughtfully .
Whoever be pull that string could n't be very big , or they would never have be able to crawl under that old board , therefore he need n't be afraid .
A gleam of mischief twinkle in Striped Chipmunk 's eye .
He seize the other end of the string and begin to pull .
Such a jerking and yanking a begin right away !
But he hold on and pull harder .
Then out from under the old board appear the queer web foot of Grandfather Frog tie together .
Striped Chipmunk be so surprised that he let go of the string and nearly fell over backward .
`` Why , Grandfather Frog , what under the sun be you do here ? ''
he shout .
When Striped Chipmunk let go of the string , Grandfather Frog promptly draw his foot back under the old board , but when he hear Striped Chipmunk 's voice , he slowly and painfully crawl out .
He tell how he have be catch and tie by Farmer Brown 's boy and finally drop near the old board .
He tell how terribly frighten he be , and how sore his leg be .
Striped Chipmunk do n't wait for him to finish .
In a flash he be at work with his sharp teeth and have cut the cruel string before Grandfather Frog have finish his story .
XVIII GRANDFATHER FROG HURRIES AWAY When Striped Chipmunk cut the string that bind the long leg of Grandfather Frog together , Grandfather Frog be so relieved that he hardly know what to do .
Of course he thank Striped Chipmunk over and over again .
Striped Chipmunk say that it be nothing , just nothing at all , and that he be very glad indeed to help Grandfather Frog .
`` We folk who live out in the Great World have to help one another , '' say Striped Chipmunk , `` because we never know when we may need help ourselves .
Now you take my advice , Grandfather Frog , and go back to the Smiling Pool as fast a you can .
The Great World be no place for an old fellow like you , because you do n't know how to take care of yourself . ''
Now when he say that , Striped Chipmunk make a great mistake .
Old people never like to be tell that they be old or that they do not know all there be to know .
Grandfather Frog straighten up and try to look very dignified .
`` Chugarum ! ''
say he , `` I 'd have you to know , Striped Chipmunk , that people be come to me for advice before you be bear .
It be just an accident that Farmer Brown 's boy catch me , and I 'd like to see him do it again .
Yes , Sir , I 'd like to see him do it again ! ''
Dear me , dear me !
Grandfather Frog be boast .
If he have be safe at home in the Smiling Pool , there might have be some excuse for boasting , but way over here in the Long Lane , not even know the way back to the Smiling Pool , it be foolish , very foolish indeed .
No one know that good than Striped Chipmunk , but he have a great deal of respect for Grandfather Frog , and he know too that Grandfather Frog be feel very much out of sort and very much mortify to think that he have be catch in such a scrape , so he put a hand over his mouth to hide a smile a he say : `` Of course he be n't go to catch you again .
I know how wise and smart you be , but you look to me very tire , and there be so many danger out here in the Great World that it seem to me that the very best thing you can do be to go back to the Smiling Pool . ''
But Grandfather Frog be stubborn , you know .
He have start out to see the Great World , and he do n't want the little people of the Green Meadows and the Green Forest to think that he be afraid .
The truth be , Grandfather Frog be more afraid of be laugh at than he be of the danger around him , which show just how foolish wise people can be sometimes .
So he shake his head .
`` Chugarum ! ''
say he , `` I be go to see the Great World first , and then I be go back to the Smiling Pool .
Do you happen to know where there be any water ?
I be very thirsty . ''
Now over on the other side of the Long Lane be a spring where Farmer Brown 's boy fill his jug with clear cold water to take with him to the cornfield when he have to work there .
Striped Chipmunk know all about that spring , for he have be there for a drink many time .
So he tell Grandfather Frog just where the spring be and how to get to it .
He even offer to show the way , but Grandfather Frog say that he would rather go alone .
`` Watch out , Grandfather Frog , and do n't fall in , because you might not be able to get out again , '' warn Striped Chipmunk .
Grandfather Frog look up sharply to see if Striped Chipmunk be make fun of him .
The very idea of any one thinking that he , who have live in the water all his life , could n't get out when he please !
But Striped Chipmunk look really in earnest , so Grandfather Frog swallow the quick retort on the tip of his tongue , thank Striped Chipmunk , and hurry away to look for the spring , for he be very , very thirsty .
Besides , he be very , very hot , and he hurry still faster a he think of the cool bath he would have when he find that spring .
XIX GRANDFATHER FROG JUMPS INTO MORE TROUBLE Some people be heedless and run into trouble .
Some people be stupid and walk into trouble .
Grandfather Frog be both heedless and stupid and jump into trouble .
When Striped Chipmunk tell him where the spring be , it seem to him that he could n't wait to reach it .
You see , Grandfather Frog have spend all his life in the Smiling Pool , where he could get a drink whenever he want it by just reach over the edge of his big green lily-pad .
Whenever he be too warm , all he have to do be to say `` Chugarum ! ''
and dive head first into the cool water .
So he be n't use to go a long time without water .
Jump , jump , jump !
Grandfather Frog be go as fast a ever he could in the direction Striped Chipmunk have point out .
Every three or four jump he would stop for just a wee , wee bit of rest , then off he would go again , jump , jump , jump !
And each jump be a long one .
Peter Rabbit certainly would have be envious if he could have see those long jump of Grandfather Frog .
At last the ground begin to grow damp .
The farther he go , the damper it grow .
Presently it become fairly wet , and there be a great deal of soft , cool , wet moss .
How good it do feel to Grandfather Frog 's poor tired foot !
`` Must be I 'm most there , '' say Grandfather Frog to himself , a he scramble up on a big mossy hummock , so a to look around .
Right away he saw a little path from the direction of the Long Lane .
It lead straight past the very hummock on which Grandfather Frog be sit , and he notice that where the ground be very soft and wet , old board have be lay down .
That puzzle Grandfather Frog a great deal .
`` It 's a sure enough path , '' say he .
`` But what under the blue , blue sky do any one want to spoil it for by put those board there ? ''
You see , Grandfather Frog like the soft wet mud , and he could n't understand how any one , even Farmer Brown 's boy , could prefer a hard dry path .
Of course he never have wear shoe himself , so he could n't understand why any one should want dry foot when they could just as well have wet one .
He be still puzzle over it when he hear a sound that make him nearly lose his balance and tumble off the hummock .
It be a whistle , the whistle of Farmer Brown 's boy !
Grandfather Frog know it right away , because he often have hear it over by the Smiling Pool .
The whistle come from over in the Long Lane .
Farmer Brown 's boy have have his dinner and be on his way back to look for Grandfather Frog where he have be drop .
Grandfather Frog actually grin a he think how surprised Farmer Brown 's boy be go to be when he could find no trace of him .
Suddenly the smile seem to freeze on Grandfather Frog 's face .
That whistle be come nearer !
Farmer Brown 's boy have leave the Long Lane and be come along the little path .
The truth be , he be come for a drink at the spring , but Grandfather Frog do n't think of this .
He be sure that in some way Farmer Brown 's boy have find out which way he have go and be come after him .
He crouch down as flat a he could on the big hummock and hold his breath .
Farmer Brown 's boy go straight past .
Just a few step beyond , he stop and kneel down .
Peeping through the grass , Grandfather Frog saw him dip up beautiful clear water in an old cup and drink .
Then Grandfather Frog know just where the spring be .
A few minute later , Farmer Brown 's boy pass again , still whistle , on his way to the Long Lane .
Grandfather Frog wait only long enough to be sure that he have really go .
Then , with big jump than ever , he start for the spring .
A dozen long jumps , and he could see the water .
Two more jump and then a long jump , and he have land in the spring with a splash !
`` Chugarum ! ''
cry Grandfather Frog .
`` How good the water feel ! ''
And all the time , Grandfather Frog have jump straight into more trouble .
XX GRANDFATHER FROG LOSES HEART Look before you leap ; The water may be deep .
That be the very best kind of advice , but most people find that out when it be too late .
Grandfather Frog do .
Of course he have hear that little verse all his life .
Indeed , he have be very fond of say it to those who come to the Smiling Pool to ask his advice .
But Grandfather Frog seem to have leave all his wisdom behind him when he leave the Smiling Pool to go out into the Great World .
You see , it be very hard work for any one whose advice have be seek to turn right around and take advice themselves .
So Grandfather Frog have be get into scrape ever since he start out on his foolish journey , and now here he be in still another , and he have land in it head first , with a great splash .
Of course , when he have see the cool , sparkling water of the spring , it have seem to him that he just could n't wait another second to get into it .
He be so hot and dry and dreadfully thirsty and uncomfortable !
And so -- oh , dear me !
-- Grandfather Frog do n't look at all before he leap .
No , Sir , he do n't !
He just dive in with a great long jump .
Oh , how good that water felt !
For a few minute he could n't think of anything else .
It be cool than the water of the Smiling Pool , because , a you know , it be a spring .
But it felt all the good for that , and Grandfather Frog just close his eye and float there in pure happiness .
Presently he open his eye to look around .
Then he blink them rapidly for a minute or so .
He rub them to make sure that he saw aright .
His heart seem to sink way , way down towards his toe .
`` Chugarum ! ''
exclaim Grandfather Frog , `` Chugarum ! ''
And after that for a long time he do n't say a word .
You see , it be this way .
All around him rise perfectly straight smooth wall .
He could look up and see a little of the blue , blue sky right overhead and whisper leaf of tree and bush .
Over the edge of the smooth straight wall grass be bend .
But they be so far above his head , so dreadfully far !
There be n't any place to climb out !
Grandfather Frog be in a prison !
He do n't understand it at all , but it be so .
Of course , Farmer Brown 's boy could have tell him all about it .
A long time before Farmer Brown himself have find that spring , and because the water be so clear and cold and pure , he have clear away all the dirt and rubbish around it .
Then he have knock the bottom out of a nice clean barrel and have dig down where the water bubble up out of the sand and have set the barrel down in this hole and have fill in the bottom with clean white sand for the water to bubble up through .
About half-way up the barrel he have cut a little hole for the water to run out as fast a it bubble in at the bottom .
Of course the water never could fill the barrel , because when it reach that hole , it run out .
This leave a straight , smooth wall up above , a wall altogether too high for Grandfather Frog to jump over from the inside .
Poor old Grandfather Frog !
He wish more than ever that he never , never have think of leave the Smiling Pool to see the Great World .
Round and round he swim , but he could n't see any way out of it .
The little hole where the water run out be too small for him to squeeze through , a he find out by try and try .
So far a he could see , he have just get to stay there all the rest of his life .
Worse still , he know that Farmer Brown 's boy sometimes come to the spring for a drink , for he have see him do it .
That mean that the very next time he come , he would find Grandfather Frog , because there be no place to hide .
When Grandfather Frog thought of that , he just lose heart .
Yes , Sir , he just lose heart .
He give up all hope of ever see the Smiling Pool again , and two big tear run out of his big goggly eye .
XXI THE MERRY LITTLE BREEZES TRY TO COMFORT GRANDFATHER FROG When the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind have leave Grandfather Frog in the Long Lane where Farmer Brown 's boy have drop him , and have hurry as fast a ever they could to try to find some of his friend to help him , not one of them have be successful .
No one be at home , and no one be in any of the place where they usually be to be find .
The Merry Little Breezes look and look .
Then , one by one , they sadly turn back to the Long Lane .
They felt so badly that they just hat to go back where they have leave Grandfather Frog .
When they get there , they find Striped Chipmunk , who now be scold Farmer Brown 's boy as fast a his tongue could go .
`` Where be he ? ''
cry the Merry Little Breezes excitedly .
Striped Chipmunk stop scold long enough to point to Farmer Brown 's boy , who be hunt in the grass for some trace of Grandfather Frog .
`` We do n't mean him , you stupid !
We can see him for ourselves .
Where 's Grandfather Frog ? ''
cry the Merry Little Breezes , all speaking at once .
`` I do n't know , '' reply Striped Chipmunk , `` and what 's more , I do n't care ! ''
Now this be n't true , for Striped Chipmunk be n't that kind .
It be mostly talk , and the Merry Little Breezes know it .
They know that Striped Chipmunk really think a great deal of Grandfather Frog , just a they do .
So they pretend not to notice what he say or how put out he seem .
After a while , he tell them that he have set Grandfather Frog free and that then he have start for the spring on the other side of the Long Lane .
The Merry Little Breezes be delight to hear the good news , and they say such a lot of nice thing to Striped Chipmunk that he quite forget to scold Farmer Brown 's boy .
Then they start for the spring , dance merrily , for they felt sure that there Grandfather Frog be all right , and they expect to find him quite at home .
`` Hello , Grandfather Frog ! ''
they shout , a they peep into the spring .
`` How do you like your new home ? ''
Grandfather Frog make no reply .
He just roll his great goggly eye up at them , and they be full of tear .
`` Why -- why -- why , Grandfather Frog , what be the matter now ? ''
they cry .
`` Chugarum , '' say Grandfather Frog , and his voice sound all choky , `` I ca n't get out . ''
Then they notice for the first time how straight and smooth the wall of the spring be and how far down Grandfather Frog be , and they know that he speak the truth .
They try bend down the grass that grow around the edge of the spring , but none be long enough to reach the water .
If they have stop to think , they would have know that Grandfather Frog could n't have climb up by them , anyway .
Then they try to lift a big stick into the spring , but it be too heavy for them , and they could n't move it .
However , they do manage to blow an old shingle in , and this give Grandfather Frog something to sit on , so that he begin to feel a little good .
Then they say all the comfort thing they could think of .
They tell him that no harm could come to him there , unless Farmer Brown 's boy should happen to see him .

croak Grandfather Frog .

`` That 's just what I be afraid of ! ''
croak Grandfather Frog .
`` He be sure to see me if he come for a drink , for there be no place for me to hide . ''
`` Perhaps he wo n't come , '' say one of the Little Breezes hopefully .
`` If he do come , you can hide under the piece of shingle , and then he wo n't know you be here at all , '' say another .
Grandfather Frog brighten up .
`` That 's so ! ''
say he .
`` That 's a good idea , and I 'll try it . ''
Then one of the Merry Little Breezes promise to keep watch for Farmer Brown 's boy , and all the others start off on another hunt for some one to help Grandfather Frog out of this new trouble .
XXII GRANDFATHER FROG 'S TROUBLES GROW Head first in ; no way out ; It 's best to know what you 're about !
Grandfather Frog have have plenty of time to realize how very true this be .
As he sit on the old shingle which the Merry Little Breezes have blow into the spring where he be a prisoner , he think a great deal about that little word `` if . ''
If he have n't leave the Smiling Pool , if he have n't be stubborn and set in his way , if he have n't be in such a hurry , if he have look to see where he be leap -- well , any one of these ifs would have keep him out of his present trouble .
It really be n't so bad in the spring .
That be , it would n't have be so bad but for the fear that Farmer Brown 's boy might come for a drink and find him there .
That be Grandfather Frog 's one great fear , and it give him bad dream whenever he try to take a nap .
He grow cold all over at the very thought of be catch again by Farmer Brown 's boy , and when at last one of the Merry Little Breezes hurry up to tell him that Farmer Brown 's boy actually be come , poor old Grandfather Frog be so frightened that the Merry Little Breeze have to tell him twice to hide under the old shingle a it float on the water .
At last he get it through his head , and draw a very long breath , he dive into the water and swam under the old shingle .
He be just in time .
Yes , Sir , he be just in time .
If Farmer Brown 's boy have n't be think of something else , he certainly would have notice the little ring on the water make by Grandfather Frog when he dive in .
But he be think of something else , and it be n't until he dip a cup in for the second time that he even saw the old shingle .
`` Hello ! ''
he exclaim .
`` That must have blow in since I be here yesterday .
We ca n't have anything like that in our nice spring . ''
With that he reach out for the old shingle , and Grandfather Frog , hide under it , give himself up for lose .
But the anxious Little Breeze have be watch sharply and the instant he saw what Farmer Brown 's boy be go to do , he play the old , old trick of snatch his hat from his head .
The truth be , he could n't think of anything else to do .
Farmer Brown 's boy grab at his hat , and then , because he be in a hurry and have other thing to do , he start off without once thinking of the old shingle again .
`` Chugarum ! ''
cry Grandfather Frog , a he swim out from under the shingle and climb up on it , `` That certainly be a close call .
If I have many more like it , I certainly shall die of fright . ''
Nothing more happen for a long time , and Grandfather Frog be wonder if it would n't be safe to take a nap when he saw peep over the edge above him two eye .
They be greenish yellow eye , and they star and star .
Grandfather Frog star and star back .
He just could n't help it .
He do n't know who they belong to .
He could n't remember ever have see them before .
He be afraid , and yet somehow he could n't make up his mind to jump .
He star so hard at the eye that he do n't notice a long furry paw slowly , very slowly , reach down towards him .
Nearer it creep and nearer .
Then suddenly it move like a flash .
Grandfather Frog felt sharp claw in his white and yellow waistcoat , and before he could even open his mouth to cry `` Chugarum , '' he be send fly through the air and land on his back in the grass .
Pounce !
Two paw pin him down , and the greenish yellow eye be not an inch from his own .
They belong to Black Pussy , Farmer Brown 's cat .
XXIII THE DEAR OLD SMILING POOL ONCE MORE Black Pussy be have a good time .
Grandfather Frog be n't .
It be great fun for Black Pussy to slip a paw under Grandfather Frog and toss him up in the air .
It be still more fun to pretend to go away , but to hide instead , and the instant Grandfather Frog start off , to pounce upon him and cuff him and roll him about .
But there be n't any fun in it for Grandfather Frog .
In the first place , he do n't know whether or not Black Pussy like Frogs to eat , and he be terribly frighten .
In the second place , Black Pussy do n't always cover up her claw , and they prick right through Grandfather Frog 's white and yellow waistcoat and hurt , for he be very tender there .
At last Black Pussy grow tire of playing , so catch up Grandfather Frog in her mouth , she start along the little path from the spring to the Long Lane .
Grandfather Frog do n't even kick , which be just as well , because if he have , Black Pussy would have hold him tight , and that would have be very uncomfortable indeed .
`` It 's all over , and this be the end , '' moan Grandfather Frog .
`` I 'm go to be eat now .
Oh , why , why do I ever leave the Smiling Pool ? ''
Just a Black Pussy slip into the Long Lane , Grandfather Frog hear a familiar sound .
It be a whistle , a merry whistle .
It be the whistle of Farmer Brown 's boy .
It be come nearer and nearer .
A little bit of hope begin to stir in the heart of Grandfather Frog .
He do n't know just why , but it do .
Always he have be in the great fear of Farmer Brown 's boy , but now -- well , if Farmer Brown 's boy should take him , he might get away from him a he do before , but he be very sure that he never , never could get away from Black Pussy .
The whistle draw nearer .
Black Pussy stop .
Then she begin to make a queer whir sound deep down in her throat .
`` Hello , Black Pussy !
Have you be hunt ?
Come here and show me what you 've get , '' cry a voice .
Black Pussy arch up her back and begin to rub against the leg of Farmer Brown 's boy , and all the time the whir , ring sound in her throat grow loud and louder .
Farmer Brown 's boy stoop down to see what she have in her mouth .
`` Why , '' he exclaim , `` I do believe this be the very same old frog that get away from me !
You do n't want him , Puss .
I 'll just put him in my pocket and take him up to the house by and by . ''
With that he take Grandfather Frog from Black Pussy and drop him in his pocket .
He pat Black Pussy , call her a smart cat , and then start on his way , whistle merrily .
It be dark and rather close in that pocket , but Grandfather Frog do n't mind this .
It be a lot good than feel sharp teeth and claw all the time .
He wonder how soon they would reach the house and what would happen to him then .
After what seem like a long , long time , he felt himself swung through the air , and then he land on the ground with a thump that make him grunt .
Farmer Brown 's boy have take off his coat and throw it down .
The whistling stop .
Everything be quiet .
Grandfather Frog wait and listen , but not a sound could he hear .
Then he saw a little ray of light creep into his prison .
He squirm and push , and all of a sudden he be out of the pocket .
The bright light make him blink .
As soon a he could see , he look to see where he be .
Then he rub his eye with both hand and look again .
He be n't at Farmer Brown 's house at all .
Where do you think he be ?
Why , right on the bank of the Smiling Pool , and a little way off be Farmer Brown 's boy fishing !
`` Chugarum ! ''
cry Grandfather Frog , and it be the loud , glad chugarum that the Smiling Pool ever have hear .
`` Chugarum ! ''
he cry again , and with a great leap he dive with a splash into the dear old Smiling Pool , which smile more than ever .
And never again have Grandfather Frog try to see the Great World .
He be quite content to leave it to those who like to dwell there .
And since his own wonderful adventure , he have be ready to believe anything he be tell about what happen there .
