CHAPTER I : Jerry Muskrat Has A Fright What be it Mother Muskrat have say about Farmer Brown 's boy and his trap ?

The fact be he could n't forget what Jerry Muskrat and Little Joe Otter have tell him -- that there be something the matter with the Smiling Pool .
He do n't believe it , not a word of it .
At least he try to make himself think that he do n't believe it .
They have say that the water in the Smiling Pool be grow low and low , just a it do in the middle of summer , in the very hot weather .
Now Grandfather Frog be very old and very wise , and he have never hear of such a thing happen in the springtime .
So he would n't believe it now .
And yet -- and yet Grandfather Frog have an uncomfortable feeling that something be wrong .
Ha !
he know now what it be !
He have be sit up to his middle in water , and now he be sit with only his toe in the water , and he could n't remember have change his position !
`` Of course , I move without think what I be do , '' mutter Grandfather Frog , but still the worried look do n't leave his face .
You see he just could n't make himself believe what he want to believe , try a he would .
`` Chugarum !
I know what I 'll do ; I 'll watch my toe ! ''
exclaim Grandfather Frog .
So Grandfather Frog wad out into the water until it cover his foot , and then he sit down and begin to watch his toe .
Mr. Redwing look down and saw him , and Grandfather Frog look so funny gazing at his own toe that Mr. Redwing stop sing long enough to ask : `` What be you do , Grandfather Frog ? ''
`` Watching my toe , '' reply Grandfather Frog gruffly .
`` Watching your toe !
Ho , ho , ho !
Watching your toe !
Who ever heard of such a thing ?
Are you afraid that they will run away , Grandfather Frog ? ''
shout Mr. Redwing .
Grandfather Frog do n't answer .
He keep right on watch his toe .
Mr. Redwing fly away to tell everybody he meet how Grandfather Frog have become foolish and be watch his toe .
The sun shine down warm and bright , and pretty soon Grandfather Frog 's big goggly eye begin to blink .
Then his head begin to nod , and then -- why , then Grandfather Frog fell fast asleep .
By and by Grandfather Frog awake with a start .
He look down at his toe .
They be not in the water at all !
Indeed , the water be a good long jump away .
`` Chugarum !
There be something wrong with the Smiling Pool ! ''
cry Grandfather Frog , a he make a long jump into the water and start to swim out to the Big Rock .
CHAPTER IX : The Laughing Brook Stops Laughing There be something wrong .
Grandfather Frog know it the very minute he get up that morning .
At first he could n't think what it be .
He sit with just his head out of water and blink his great goggly eye , a he try to think what it be that be wrong .
Suddenly Grandfather Frog realize how still it be .
It be a different kind of stillness from anything he could ever remember .
He miss something , and he could n't think what it be .
It be n't the song of Mr. Redwing .
There be many time when he do n't hear that .
It be -- Grand-father Frog give a startled jump out on to the shore .
`` Chugarum !
It 's the Laughing Brook !
The Laughing Brook have stop laugh ! ''
cry Grandfather Frog .
Could it be ?
Who ever heard of such a thing , except when Jack Frost bound the Laughing Brook with hard black ice ?
Why , in the spring and in the summer and in the fall the Laughing Brook have laugh -- such a merry , happy laugh -- ever since Grandfather Frog could remember , and you know he can remember way back in the long ago , for he be very old and very wise .
Never once in all that time have the Laughing Brook fail to laugh .
It could n't be true now !
Grandfather Frog put a hand behind one ear and listen and listen , but not a sound could he hear .
`` Chugarum !
It must be me , '' say Grandfather Frog .
`` It must be that I be grow old and deaf .
I 'll go over and ask Jerry Muskrat . ''
So Grandfather Frog dive into the water and swam out to the middle of the Smiling Pool , on his way to Jerry Muskrat 's house .
It be then that he first fully realize the truth of what Jerry Muskrat and Little Joe Otter have tell him the day before -- that there be something very , very wrong with the Smiling Pool .
He stop swim to look around , and it seem a if his great goggly eye would pop right out of his head .
Yes , Sir , it seem a if those great goggly eye certainly would pop right out of Grandfather Frog 's head .
The Smiling Pool have grow so small that there be n't enough of it leave to smile !
`` Where be you go , Grandfather Frog ? ''
ask a voice over his head .
Grandfather Frog look up .
Looking down on him from over the edge of the Big Rock be Jerry Muskrat .
The edge of the Big Rock be twice as high above the water a Grandfather Frog have ever see it before .

demand Grandfather Frog in great surprise .

`` What 's that you say ? ''
cry Grandfather Frog , a if he could n't believe his own ear .
`` It 's just as true a that I 'm sit here , '' reply Jerry sadly .
`` Listen , Jerry Muskrat , and tell me truly ; be the Laughing Brook laugh ? ''

`` No , '' reply Jerry , `` the Laughing Brook have stop laugh , and the Smiling Pool have stop smile , and I think the world be upside down . ''
CHAPTER X : Why The World Seemed Upside Down To Jerry Muskrat Jerry Muskrat sit on the Big Rock in the Smiling Pool , which smile no longer , and hold his head in both hand , for his head ache .
He have think and think and think , until it seem to him that his head would split ; and with all his thinking , he do n't understand thing any more now than he have in the beginning .
You see , Jerry Muskrat 's little world be topsy-turvy .
Yes , Sir , Jerry 's world be upside down !
Anyway , it seem so to him , and he could n't understand it at all .
The Smiling Pool , the Laughing Brook , and the Green Meadows be Jerry Muskrat 's little world .
Now , a he sit on the Big Rock and look about him , the Green Meadows be as lovely a ever .
He could see no change in them .
But the Laughing Brook have stop laugh , and the Smiling Pool have stop smile .
The truth be there be n't enough of the Laughing Brook leave to laugh , and there be n't enough of the Smiling Pool leave to smile .
It be dreadful !
Jerry look over to his house , of which he have once be so proud .
He have build it with the doorway under water .
He have felt perfectly safe there , because no one except Billy Mink or Little Joe Otter , who can swim under water , could reach him .

Anybody who want to could get into it .
There be the doorway plainly to be see .
Worse still , there be the secret entrance to the long tunnel lead to his castle under the root of the Big Hickory-tree .
That have be Jerry 's most secret secret , and now there it be for all the world to see .
And there be all the wonderful cave and hole and hiding-places under the bank which have be know only to Jerry Muskrat and Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter , because the opening have always be under water .
Now anybody could find them , for they be plainly to be see .
And where have always be smile , dimple water , Jerry saw only mud .
It be mud , mud , mud everywhere !
The bulrush , which have always grow with their foot in the water , now have them only in mud , and that be fast dry up .
The lily-pads lay half curl up at the end of their long stem , stretch out on the mud , and look very , very sick .
Jerry turn towards the Laughing Brook .
There be just a little , teeny , weeny stream of water trickle down the middle of it , with here and there a tiny pool in which frighten trout and minnow be crowd .
All the secret of the Laughing Brook be expose , just a be the secret of the Smiling Pool .
Jerry know that if he want to find Billy Mink 's hiding-places , all he need do would be to walk up the Laughing Brook and look .
`` Yes , Sir , the world have turn upside down , '' say Jerry in a mournful voice .
`` I believe it have , '' reply Grandfather Frog , look up from the little pool of water leave at the foot of the Big Rock .
`` I know it have ! ''
cry Jerry .
`` I wonder if it will ever turn upside up again . ''

ask Grandfather Frog .
`` I do n't know , '' reply Jerry Muskrat .
`` Here come Little Joe Otter and Billy Mink ; let 's find out what they be go to do . ''
CHAPTER XI : Five Heads Together Something have to be do .
Jerry Muskrat say so .
Grandfather Frog say so .
Billy Mink say so .
Little Joe Otter say so .
Even Spotty the Turtle say so .
The Laughing Brook could n't laugh , and the Smiling Pool could n't smile .

Nobody have ever know anything like it before , and so nobody know what to think or do .
And yet they all felt that something must be do .

But somehow he do n't want to catch them .
He know that they be frighten almost to death already by the run away of nearly all the water from the Laughing Brook and the Smiling Pool , and somehow he felt sorry for them .

`` Chugarum !

`` There 's nothing happen , a you know , But have a cause to make it so .
`` Now there must be some cause , some reason , for this terrible trouble with the Smiling Pool , and if we can find that out , perhaps we shall know good what to do , '' say Grandfather Frog .

`` Chugarum ! ''

`` Well , that 's where the cause of all the trouble be , '' say Grandfather Frog , just a if he know all about it .

Let u all go , '' say Grandfather Frog .

CHAPTER XII : A Hunt For Trouble Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , sail high in the blue , blue sky , look down on a funny sight .
Yes , Sir , it certainly be a funny sight .
It be a little procession of five of his friend of the Smiling Pool .
First be Billy Mink , who , because he be slim and nimble , move so quickly it sometimes be hard to follow him .
Behind him be Little Joe Otter , whose leg be so short that he almost look a if he have n't any .
Behind Little Joe be Jerry Muskrat , who be a good traveler in the water than on land .
Behind Jerry be Grandfather Frog , who neither walk nor run but travel with great jump .
Last of all be Spotty the Turtle , who travel very , very slowly because , you know , he carry his house with him .
And all five be head up the Laughing Brook , which laugh no more , because there be not water enough in it .
Now Ol ' Mistah Buzzard have n't be over near the Smiling Pool for some time , and he have n't hear how the Smiling Pool have stop smile , and the Laughing Brook have stop laugh .
When he look down and saw how the water be so nearly go from them that the trout and the minnow have hardly enough in which to live , he be so surprised that he keep say over and over to himself : `` Fo ' the lan 's sake !
Fo ' the lan 's sake ! ''
Then , when he saw his five little friend march up the Laughing Brook , he guess right away that it must be something to do with the trouble in the Smiling Pool .
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard just turn his broad wing and slide down , down out of the blue , blue sky until he be right over Grandfather Frog .
`` Where be yo'alls go ? ''
ask Ol ' Mistah Buzzard .
`` Chugarum !
To find out what be the trouble with the Laughing Brook , '' reply Grandfather Frog .

Grandfather Frog watch him until he be nothing but a speck .
`` I wish I have wing , '' sigh Grandfather Frog , and once more begin to hop along up the bed of the Laughing Brook .
The Laughing Brook come down from the Green Forest and wind through the Green Meadows for a little way before it reach the Smiling Pool .
There the sun shone down into it , and Grandfather Frog do n't mind , although his leg be get tire .
But when they get into the Green Forest it be dark and gloomy .
At least Grandfather Frog think so , and so do Spotty the Turtle , for both dearly love the sunshine .

If they find this , they would also find the trouble with the Smiling Pool .
So Billy Mink jump and skip far ahead ; Little Joe Otter run ; Jerry Muskrat walk , for he soon get tire on land ; Grandfather Frog hop ; Spotty the Turtle crawl , and way , way up in the blue , blue sky , OF Mistah Buzzard fly , all look for the trouble which have stop the laughing of the Laughing Brook and the smiling of the Smiling Pool .
CHAPTER XIII : Ol ' Mistah Buzzard Sees Something `` Wait for me ! ''
cry Little Joe Otter to Billy Mink , but Billy Mink be in too much of a hurry and just run faster .

So running and walking and jumping and crawling , Billy Mink , Little Joe Otter , Jerry Muskrat , Grandfather Frog , and Spotty the Turtle hurry up the Laughing Brook to try to find out why it laugh no more .
And high overhead in the blue , blue sky sail Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , and he also be look for the trouble that have take away the laugh from the Laughing Brook and the smile from the Smiling Pool .
Now Ol ' Mistah Buzzard 's eye be very sharp , and look down from way up in the blue , blue sky he can see a great deal .
Indeed , Ol ' Mistah Buzzard can see all that be go on below on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest .

Now , a he look down , he saw that Billy Mink be selfish and would n't wait for Little Joe Otter , and Little Joe Otter be selfish and would n't wait for Jerry Muskrat , and Jerry Muskrat be selfish and would n't wait for Grandfather Frog , and Grandfather Frog be selfish and would n't wait for Spotty the Turtle .
`` Ah reckon Ah will hurry up right smart and find out what the trouble be mahself , and then go back and tell Brer Turtle ; it will save him a powerful lot of work , and it will serve Brer Mink right if Brer Turtle find out first what be the trouble with the Laughing Brook , '' say Ol ' Mistah Buzzard and shot far ahead over the Green Forest towards that part of it from which the Laughing Brook come .
In a few minute he be a far ahead of Billy Mink a Billy be ahead of Spotty the Turtle .
For wing be swifter far than leg , On whatsoever purpose bent , But doubly swift and tireless Those wing on kindly deed intent .

He forget everything but his own great surprise , and he blink his eye a great many time to make sure that he be n't dream .

No , Ah never !
Did yo ' ever ?
No , Ah never ! ''
CHAPTER XIV : Spotty The Turtle Keeps Right On Going `` One step , two step , three step , so !
Four step , five step , six step go !
Keep right on and do your best ; Mayhap you 'll win while others rest . ''
Spotty the Turtle say this over to himself every time he felt a little down-hearted , a he plod along the bed of the Laughing Brook .
And every time he say it , he felt well .
`` One step , two step , '' he keep say over and over , and each time he say it , he take a step and then another .
They be very short step , very short step indeed , for Spotty 's leg be very short .
But each one carry him forward just so much , and he know that he be just so much nearer the thing he be seek .
Anyway , he hop he be .
You see , if the Laughing Brook would never laugh any more , and the Smiling Pool would never smile any more , there be nothing to do but to go down to the Big River to live , and no one want to do that , especially Grandfather Frog and Spotty the Turtle .
Now , because Billy Mink could go faster than Little Joe Otter , and Little Joe Otter could go faster than Jerry Muskrat , and Jerry could go faster than Grandfather Frog , and Grandfather Frog could go faster than Spotty the Turtle , and because each one want to be the first to find the trouble , no one would wait for the one behind him .
So Spotty the Turtle , who have to carry his house with him , be a long , long way behind the others .
But he keep right on go .
`` One step , two step , three step , so ! ''
and he do n't stop for anything .
He crawl over stick and around big stone and sometimes , when he find a little pool of water , he swim .
He always felt well then , because he can swim fast than he can walk .
After a long , long time , Spotty the Turtle come to a little pool where the sunshine lay warm and inviting .
There , in the middle of it , on a mossy stone , sit Grandfather Frog fast asleep .
He have think that he be so far ahead of Spotty that he could safely rest his tired leg .
Spotty want to climb right up beside him and take a nap too , but he do n't .
He just grin and keep right on go .
`` One step , two step , three step , so ! ''
while Grandfather Frog sleep on .
By and by , after a long , long time Spotty come to another little pool , and who should he see but Jerry Muskrat busily open and eat some freshwater clam which he have find there .
He be so busy enjoy himself that he do n't see Spotty , and Spotty do n't say a word , but keep right on go , although the sight of Jerry 's feast have make him dreadfully hungry .
By and by , after a long , long time , he come to a third little pool with a high , smooth bank , and who should he see there but Little Joe Otter , who have make a slippery slide down the smooth bank and be have a glorious time slide down into the little pool .
Spotty would have like to take just one slide , but he do n't .
He do n't even let Little Joe Otter see him , but keep right on go .
`` One step , two step , three step , so ! ''
By and by , after a long , long time , he come to a hollow log , and just happen to peep in , he saw some one curl up fast asleep .
Who be it ?
Why , Billy Mink , to be sure !
You see , Billy think that he be so far ahead that he might just as well take it easy , and that be what he be do .
Spotty the Turtle do n't waken him .
He just keep right on go the same slow way he have come all day , and so , just a jolly , round , red Mr. Sun be go to bed behind the Purple Hills , Spotty the Turtle find the cause of the trouble in the Laughing Brook and the Smiling Pool .
CHAPTER XV : What Spotty The Turtle Found Spotty the Turtle star and star and star , until it seem a if his eye surely would pop out of his funny little head .
Of course he could believe his own eye , and yet -- and yet -- well , if anybody else have see what he be look at and have tell him about it , he would n't have believe it .
No , Sir , he would n't have believe it .
You see , he could n't have believe it because -- why , because it do n't seem a if it could be really and truly so .
He wonder if the sun shin in his eye make him think he saw more than he really do see , so he carefully change his position .
It make no difference .
Then Spotty be sure that what he saw be real , and that he have find the cause of the trouble in the Laughing Brook , which have make it stop laughing and the Smiling Pool stop smile .
Spotty the Turtle be feel pretty good .
In fact , Spotty be feel very good indeed , because he have be the first to find out what be the matter with the Laughing Brook .
At least , he think that he be the first , and he be of all the little people who live in the Smiling Pool .

Little Joe Otter have stop to play .
Jerry Muskrat have stop to eat .
Grandfather Frog have stop for a sun-nap .

Do you wonder that he felt proud and very happy ?
Keeping at it , that 's the way Spotty win the race that day .
But now Spotty be begin to wish that some of the others would hurry up .
He want to know what they think .
He want to talk it all over .
It be such a surprising thing that he could make neither head nor tail of it himself , and he wonder what the others would say .
And now the long black shadow be creep through the Green Forest , and if they do n't get there pretty soon , they would have to wait until the next day .
So Spotty the Turtle find a good place to spend the night , and then he sit down to watch and wait .
Right before him be the thing which he have find and which puzzle him so .
What be it ?
Why , it be a wall .
Yes , Sir , that be just what it be -- a wall of log and stick and mud , and it be right across the Laughing Brook , where the bank be steep and narrow .
Of course the Laughing Brook could laugh no longer ; there could n't enough water get through that wall of log and stick and mud to make even the beginning of a laugh .
Spotty wonder what lay behind that wall , and who have build it , and what for , and a lot of other thing .
And he be still wonder when he fell asleep .
CHAPTER XVI : The Pond In The Green Forest SPOTTY THE TURTLE be awake by the time the first ray of the rise sun begin to creep through the Green Forest .
He be far , far up the Laughing Brook , very much farther than he have ever be before , and a he yawn and stretch , he wonder if after all he have n't dream about the wall of log and stick and mud across the Laughing Brook .
When he have rub the last sleepy-wink out of his eye , he look again .
There it be , just a he have see it the night before !
Then Spotty know that it be real , and he begin to wonder what be on the other side of it .
`` I can not climb it , for my leg be never make for climb , '' say Spotty mournfully a he look at his funny little black foot .
`` Oh , dear , I wish that I could climb like Happy Jack Squirrel ! ''
Just then a thought pop into his head and chase away the little frown that have creep into Spotty 's face .
`` Perhaps Happy Jack sometimes wish that he could swim a I can , so I guess we be even .
I ca n't climb , but he ca n't swim .
How foolish it be to wish for thing never mean for you ! ''
And with that , all the discontent leave Spotty the Turtle , and he begin to study how he could make the most of his short leg and his perseverance , of which , a you already know , he have a great deal .
He look this way , and he look that way , and he saw that if he could climb to the top of the bank on one side of the Laughing Brook , he would be able to walk right out on the strange wall of log and stick and mud , and then , of course , he could see just what be on the other side .
So Spotty the Turtle waste no more time wishing that he could do something it be never mean that he should do .
Instead , he pick out what look like the easy place to climb the bank and start up .
My , my , my , it be hard work !
You see , he have to carry his house along with him , for he have to carry that wherever he go , and it would have be hard enough to have climbed that bank without carry anything .
Every time he have climb up three step he slip back two step , but he keep at it , puff and blowing , say over and over to himself : `` I can if I will , and will if I can !
I 'm sure to get there if I follow this plan . ''
Half-way up the bank Spotty lose his balance , and the house he be carry just tip him right over backward , and down he roll to the place he have start from .
`` I need to cool off , '' say Spotty to himself and slide into a little pool of water .
Then he try the bank again , and just a before he slip back two step for every three he go up .
But he shut his mouth tight and kept at it , and by and by he be up to the place from which he have tumble .
There he stop to get his breath .
`` I can if I will , and will if I can !
I 'm sure to get there if I follow this plan , '' say he and start on again .
Twice more he tumble clear down to the place he have start from , but each time he laugh at himself and try again .
And at last he reach the top of the bank .
`` I say I could if I would , and I would if I could , and I have ! ''
he cry .
Then he hurry to see what be behind the strange wall .
What do you think it be ?
Why , a pond !
Yes , Sir , there be a pond right in the middle of the Green Forest !
Trees be come up right out of the middle of it , but it be a sure enough pond .
Spotty find it hard work to believe his own eye now than when he have first see the strange wall across the Laughing Brook .
`` Why , why , why , what do it mean ? ''
exclaim Spotty the Turtle .
`` That 's what I want to know ! ''
cry Billy Mink , who come hurry up just then .
CHAPTER XVII : Who Had Made The Strange Pond ?
Who have make the strange pond ?
That be what Spotty the Turtle want to know .
That be what Billy Mink want to know .
So do Little Joe Otter and Jerry Muskrat and Grandfather Frog , when they arrive .
So do Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , look down from the blue , blue sky .
It be very strange , very strange indeed !
Never have there be a pond in that part of the Green Forest before , not even in the day when Sister South Wind melt the snow so fast that the Laughing Brook run over it bank and the Smiling Pool grow twice as large a it ought to be .
Of course some one have make it .
Spotty the Turtle have know that as soon a he have see the strange pond .
All in a flash he have understand what that wall of log and brush and mud across the Laughing Brook be for .
It be to stop the water from run down the Laughing Brook .
And of course , if the water could n't keep on run and laugh on it way to the Smiling Pool , it would just stand still and grow and grow into a pond .
Of course !
There be nothing else for it to do .
Spotty felt very proud when he have think that out all by himself .
`` This wall we be sit on have make the pond , '' say Spotty the Turtle , after a long time in which no one have speak .
`` You do n't say so ! ''
say Billy Mink .
`` How ever , ever , do you guess it ?
Are you sure , quite sure that the pond do n't make the wall ? ''
Spotty know that Billy Mink be make fun of him , but he be too good-natured to lose his temper over a little thing like that .
He try to think of something smart to say in reply , but Spotty be a slow thinker as well a a slow walker , and before he could think of anything , Billy be talk once more .
`` This wall be what Farmer Brown 's boy call a dam , '' say Billy Mink , who be a great traveler .
`` Dams be usually build to keep water from run where it be n't want or to make it go where it be want .
Now , what I want to know be , who under the sun want a pond way back here in the Green Forest , and what be it for ?
Who do you think build this dam , Grandfather Frog ? ''
Grandfather Frog shake his head .
His big goggly eye seem more goggly than ever , a he star at the new pond in the Green Forest .
`` I do n't know , '' say Grandfather Frog .
`` I do n't know what to think . ''
`` Why , it must be Farmer Brown 's boy or Farmer Brown himself , '' say Jerry Muskrat .
`` Of course , '' say Little Joe Otter , just a if he know all about it .
Still Grandfather Frog shake his head , a if he do n't agree .
`` I do n't know , '' say Grandfather Frog , `` I do n't know .
It do n't look so to me . ''
Billy Mink run along the top of the dam and down the back side .
He look it all over with those sharp little eye of his .
`` Grandfather Frog be right , '' say he , when he come back .
`` It do n't look like the work of Farmer Brown or Farmer Brown 's boy .
But if they do n't do it , who do ?
Who could have do it ? ''
`` I do n't know , '' say Grandfather Frog again , in a dreamy sort of voice .
Spotty the Turtle look at him , and saw that Grandfather Frog 's face wear the far-away look that it always do when he tell a story of the day when the world be young .
`` I do n't know , '' he repeat , `` but it look to me very much like the work of -- '' Grandfather Frog stop short off and turn to Jerry Muskrat .
`` Jerry Muskrat , '' say he , so sharply that Jerry nearly lose his balance in his surprise , `` have your big cousin come down from the North ? ''
CHAPTER XVIII : Jerry Muskrat 's Big Cousin Fiddle , faddle , feedle , fuddle !
Was there ever such a muddle ?
Fuddle , feedle , faddle , fiddle !
Who be there will solve the riddle ?
Here be the Laughing Brook laugh no longer .
Here be the Smiling Pool smile no longer .
Here be a brand new pond deep in the Green Forest .
Here be a wall of log and bush and mud call a dam , build by some one whom nobody have see .
And here be Grandfather Frog ask Jerry Muskrat if his big cousin have come down from the North , when Jerry do n't even know that he have a big cousin .
`` I -- I have n't any big cousin , '' say Jerry , when he have quite recover from his surprise at Grandfather Frog 's question .
`` Chugarum ! ''
exclaim Grandfather Frog , and the scornful way in which he say it make Jerry Muskrat feel very small .
`` Chugarum !
Of course you 've get a big cousin in the North .
Do you mean to tell me that you do n't know that , Jerry Muskrat ? ''
Jerry have to admit that it be true that he do n't know anything about that big cousin .
If Grandfather Frog say that he have one , it must be so , for Grandfather Frog be very old and very wise , and he know a great deal .
Still , it be very hard for Jerry to believe that he have a big cousin of whom he have never hear .
`` Did -- do you ever see him , Grandfather Frog ? ''
Jerry ask .
`` No ! ''
snap Grandfather Frog .
`` I never do , but I know all about him .
He be a great worker , be this big cousin of yours , and he build dam like this one we be sit on . ''
`` I do n't believe it ! ''
cry Billy Mink .
`` I do n't believe any cousin of Jerry Muskrat 's ever build such a dam a this .
Why , just look at that great tree trunk at the bottom !
No one but Farmer Brown or Farmer Brown 's boy could ever have drag that there .
You 're crazy , Grandfather Frog , just plain crazy . ''
Billy Mink sometimes be very disrespectful to Grandfather Frog .
`` Chugarum ! ''
reply Grandfather Frog .
`` I 'm pretty old , but I 'm not too old to learn a some folk seem to be , '' and he look very hard at Billy Mink .
`` Did I say that that tree trunk be drag here ? ''
`` No , '' reply Billy Mink , `` but if it be n't drag here , how do it get here ?
You be so smart , Grandfather Frog , tell me that ! ''
Grandfather Frog blink his great goggly eye at Billy Mink a he say , just a if he be very , very sorry for Billy , `` Your eye be very bright and very sharp , Billy Mink , and it be a great pity that you have never learn how to use them .
That tree be n't drag here ; it be cut so that it fell right where it lie . ''
As he speak , Grandfather Frog point to the stump of the tree , and Billy Mink saw that he be right .
But Billy Mink be like a great many other people ; he dearly love to have the last word .
Now he suddenly begin to laugh .
`` Ha , ha , ha !
Ho , ho , ho ! ''
laugh Billy Mink .
`` Ho , ho , ho !
Ha , ha , ha ! ''
`` What be it that be so funny ? ''
snap Grandfather Frog , for nothing make him so angry a to be laugh at .
`` Do you mean to say that anybody but Farmer Brown or Farmer Brown 's boy could have cut down such a big tree a that ? ''
ask Billy .
`` Why , that would be as hard a to drag the tree here . ''
`` Jerry Muskrat 's big cousin from the North could do it , and I believe he do , '' reply Grandfather Frog .
`` Now that we have find the cause of the trouble in the Laughing Brook and the Smiling Pool , what be we go to do about it ? ''
CHAPTER XIX : Jerry Muskrat Has A Busy Day There be the strange pond in the Green Forest , and there be the dam of log and stick and mud which have make the strange pond , but look a they would , Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter and Jerry Muskrat and Grandfather Frog and Spotty the Turtle could see nothing of the one who have build the dam .
It be very queer .
The more they think about it , the queerer it seem .
They look this way , and they look that way .
`` There be one thing very sure , and that be that whoever build this dam have no thought for those who live in the Laughing Brook and the Smiling Pool , '' say Grandfather Frog .
`` They be selfish , just plain , every-day selfish ; that 's what they be !
Now the Laughing Brook can not laugh , and the Smiling Pool can not smile , while this dam stop the water from run , and so -- '' Grandfather Frog stop and look around at his four friend .
`` And so what ? ''
cry Billy Mink impatiently .
`` And so we must spoil this dam .
We must make a place for the water to run through , '' say Grandfather Frog very gravely .
`` Of course !
That 's the very thing ! ''
cry Little Joe Otter and Billy Mink and Jerry Muskrat and Spotty the Turtle .
Then Little Joe Otter look at Billy Mink , and Billy Mink look at Jerry Muskrat , and Jerry Muskrat look at Spotty the Turtle , and after that they all look very hard at Grandfather Frog , and all together they ask : `` How be we go to do it ? ''
Grandfather Frog scratch his head thoughtfully and look a long time at the dam of log and stick and mud .
Then his big mouth widen in a big smile .
`` Why , that be very simple , '' say he , `` Jerry Muskrat will make a big hole through the dam near the bottom , because he know how , and the rest of u will keep watch to see that no harm come near . ''
`` The very thing ! ''
cry Little Joe Otter and Billy Mink and Spotty the Turtle , but Jerry Muskrat think it be n't fair .
You see , it give him all of the real work to do .
However , Jerry thought of his dear Smiling Pool , and how terrible it would be if it should smile no more , and so without another word he set to work .
Now Jerry Muskrat be a great worker , and he have make many long tunnel into the bank around the Smiling Pool , so he have no doubt but that he could soon make a hole through this dam .
But almost right away he find trouble .
Yes , Sir , Jerry have hardly begin before he find real trouble .
You see , that dam be make mostly of stick instead of mud , and so , instead of dig his way in a he would have do into the bank of the Smiling Pool , he have to stop every few minute to gnaw off stick that be in the way .
It be hard work , the hard kind of hard work .
But Jerry Muskrat be the kind that be the more determined to do the work the hard the work be to be do .
And so , while Grandfather Frog sit on one end of the dam and pretend to keep watch , but really take a nap in the warm sunshine , and while Spotty the Turtle sit on the other end of the dam do the same thing , and while Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter swam around in the strange pond and enjoy themselves , Jerry Muskrat work and work and work .
And just a jolly , round , red Mr. Sun start down behind the Purple Hills , Jerry break through into the strange pond , and the water begin to run in the Laughing Brook once more .
CHAPTER XX : Jerry Has A Dreadful Disappointment There 's nothing in this world that 's sure , No matter how we scheme and plan .
We simply have to be content With do just the best we can .
Jerry Muskrat have curl himself up for the night , so tire that he could hardly keep his eye open long enough to find a comfortable place to sleep .
But he be happy .
Yes , indeed , Jerry be happy .
He could hear the Laughing Brook begin to laugh again .
It be just a little low , gurgle laugh , but Jerry know that in a little while it would grow into the full laugh that make music through the Green Forest and put happiness into the heart of all who hear it .
So Jerry be happy , for be it not because of him that the Laughing Brook be begin to laugh ?
He have work all the long day to make a hole through the dam which some one have build across the Laughing Brook and so stop it laughter .
Now the water be run again , and soon the new , strange pond behind the dam there in the Green Forest would be go , and the Laughing Brook and the Smiling Pool would be their own beautiful self once more .
It be because he have work so hard all day that he be go to sleep now .
Usually he would rather sleep a part of the day and be abroad at night .
Very pleasant dream have Jerry Muskrat that night , dream of the dear Smiling Pool , smile just a it have as long a Jerry could remember , before this trouble have come .
He be still dream when Spotty the Turtle find him and wake him , for it be broad daylight .
Jerry yawn and stretch , and then he lay still for a minute to listen to the pleasant murmur of the Laughing Brook .
But there be n't any pleasant murmur .
There be n't any sound at all .
Jerry begin to wonder if he really be awake after all .
He look at Spotty the Turtle , and he know then that he be , for Spotty 's face have such a worried look .
`` Get up , Jerry Muskrat , and come look at the hole you make yesterday in the dam .
You could n't have do your work very well , for the hole have fill up so that the water do not run any more , '' say Spotty .
`` I do do it well ! ''
snap Jerry crossly .
`` I do it just as well a I know how .
You lazy folk who just sit and take sun-naps while you pretend to keep watch have good get busy and do a little work yourselves , if you do n't like the way I work . ''
`` I -- I beg your pardon , Jerry Muskrat .
I do n't mean to say just that , '' reply Spotty .
`` You see , we be all worried .
We think last night that by this morning the Laughing Brook would be full of water again , and we could go back to the Smiling Pool as soon a we felt like it , and here it be as bad a ever . ''
`` Perhaps the trouble be just that some stick and grass drift down in the water and fill up the hole I make ; that must be the trouble , '' say Jerry hopefully , a he hurry towards the dam .
First he carefully examine it from the Laughing Brook side .
Then he dive down under water on the other side .
He be go a long time , and Billy Mink be just get ready to dive to see what have become of him when he come up again .
`` What be the trouble ? ''
cry Spotty the Turtle and Grandfather Frog and Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter together .
`` Is the hole fill up with stuff that have drift in ? ''
Jerry shake his head , a he slowly climb out of the water .
`` No , '' say he .
`` No , it be n't fill with drift stuff bring down by the water .
It be fill with stick and mud that somebody have put there .
Somebody have fill up the hole that I work so hard to make yesterday , and it will take me all day to open it up again . ''
Then Grandfather Frog and Spotty the Turtle and Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter and Jerry Muskrat star at one mother , and for a long time no one say a word .
CHAPTER XXI : Jerry Muskrat Keeps Watch `` The way in which to find thing out , And what go on all round about , Is just to keep my two eye peel And two ear all the time unsealed . ''
So say Jerry Muskrat , a he settle himself comfortably on one end of the new dam across the Laughing Brook deep in the Green Forest and watch the dark shadow creep far and farther out into the strange pond make by the new dam .
`` I 'm go to find out who it be that built this dam , and who it be that fill the hole I make in it !
I 'm go to find out if I have to move up here and live all summer ! ''
The way in which Jerry say this and snap his teeth together show that he mean just what he say .
You see Jerry have spend another long , weary day open the hole in the dam once more , only to have it close again while he sleep .
That have be enough for Jerry .
He have n't try again .
Instead he have make up his mind that he would find out who be play such a trick on him .
He would just watch until they come , and then if they be not big than he , or there be not too many of them , he would -- well , the way Jerry grit and clash those sharp teeth of his sound a if he mean to do something pretty bad .
Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter have give up in disgust and start for the Big River .
They be great traveler , anyway , and so do n't mind so much because there be no longer water enough in the Laughing Brook and the Smiling Pool .
Grandfather Frog and Spotty the Turtle , who be such very , very slow traveler , have decide that the Big River be too far away , and so they would stay and live in the strange pond for a while , though it be n't nearly so nice a their dear Smiling Pool .
They bad go to sleep now , each in his own secret place where he would be safe for the night .
So Jerry Muskrat sit alone and watch .
The black shadow creep far and far across the pond and grow blacker and blacker .
Jerry do n't mind this , because , a you know , his eye be make for see in the dark , and he dearly love the night .
Jerry have sit there a long time without move .
He be listen and watch .
By and by he saw something that make him draw in his breath and anger leap into his eye .
It be a little silver line on the water , and it be come straight towards the dam where he sit .
Jerry know that it be make by some one swimming .
`` Ha ! ''
say Jerry .
`` Now we shall see ! ''
Nearer and nearer come the silver line .
Then Jerry make out the head of the swimmer .
Suddenly all the anger leave Jerry .
He do n't have room for anger ; a great fear have crowd it out .
The head be big than that of any Muskrat Jerry have ever see .
It be big than the head of any of Billy Mink 's relative .
It be the head of a stranger , a stranger so big that Jerry felt very , very small and hop with all his might that the stranger would not see him .
Jerry hold his breath a the stranger swam past and then climb out on the dam .
He look very much like Jerry himself , only ever and ever so much big .
And his tail !
Jerry have never see such a tail .
It be very broad and flat .
Suddenly the big stranger turn and look straight at Jerry .
`` Hello , Jerry Muskrat ! ''
say he .
`` Do n't you know me ? ''
Jerry be too frighten to speak .
`` I 'm your big cousin from the North ; I 'm Paddy the Beaver , and if you leave my dam alone , I think we 'll be good friend , '' continue the stranger .
`` I -- I -- I hope so , '' say Jerry in a very faint voice , try to be polite , but with his teeth chatter with fear .
CHAPTER XXII : Jerry Loses His Fear `` Oh , tell me , you and you and you , If it may hap you 've ever hear Of all that wond ` rous be and great The great be the spoken word ? ''
It 's true .
It 's the true thing that ever be .
If you do n't believe it , you just go ask Jerry Muskrat .
He 'll tell you it 's true , and Jerry know .
You see , it 's this way : Words be more than just sound .
Oh , my , yes !
They be little messenger , and once they have be send out , you ca n't call them back .
No , Sir , you ca n't call them back , and sometimes that be a very sad thing , because -- well , you see these little messenger always carry something to some one else , and that something may be anger or hate or fear or an untruth , and it be these thing which make most of the trouble in this world .
Or that something may be love or sympathy or helpfulness or kindness , and it be these thing which put an end to most of the trouble in this world .
Just take the ease of Jerry Muskrat .
There he sit on the new dam , which have make the strange pond in the Green Forest , shake with fear until his teeth chatter , a he watch a stranger very , very much big than he climb up on the dam .
Jerry be afraid , because he have see that the stranger could swim as well a he could , and a Jerry have no secret burrow there , he know that he could n't get away from the stranger if he want to .
Somehow , Jerry know without be tell that the stranger have build the dam , and you know Jerry have twice make a hole in the dam to let the water out of the strange pond into the Laughing Brook .
Jerry know right down in his heart that if he have build that dam , he would be very , very angry with any one who try to spoil it , and that be just what he have try to do .
So he sit with chatter teeth , too frighten to even try to run .
`` I wish I have let some one else keep watch , '' say Jerry to himself .
Then the big stranger have speak .
He have say : `` Hello , Jerry Muskrat !
Do n't you know me ? ''
and his voice have n't sound the least bit angry .
Then he have tell Jerry that he be his big cousin , Paddy the Beaver , and he hop that they would be friend .
Now everything be just a it have be before -- the strange pond , the dam , Jerry himself and the big stranger , and the black shadow of the night -- and yet somehow , everything be different , all because a few pleasant word have be speak .
A great fear have fall away from Jerry 's heart , and in it place be a great hope that after all there be n't to be any trouble .
So he reply to Paddy the Beaver as politely a he know how .
Paddy be just a polite , and the first thing Jerry know , instead of be enemy , a Jerry have all along make up his mind would be the case when he find the builder of the dam , here they be become the best of friend , all because Paddy the Beaver have say the right thing in the right way .
`` But you have n't tell me yet what you make those hole in my dam for , Cousin Jerry , '' say Paddy the Beaver finally .
Jerry do n't know just what to say .
He be so pleased with his big new cousin that he do n't want to hurt his feeling by tell him that he do n't think that dam have any business to be across the Laughing Brook , and at the same time he want Paddy to know how he have spoil the Laughing Brook and the Smiling Pool .
At last he make up his mind to tell the whole story .
CHAPTER XXIII : Paddy The Beaver Does A Kind Deed Paddy the Beaver listen to all that his small cousin , Jerry Muskrat , have to tell him about the trouble which Paddy 's dam have cause in the Laughing Brook and the Smiling Pool .
`` You see , we who live in the Smiling Pool love it dearly , and we do n't want to have to leave it , but if the water can not run down the Laughing Brook , there can be no Smiling Pool , and so we will have to move off to the Big River , '' conclude Jerry Muskrat .
`` That be why I try to spoil your dam . ''
There be a twinkle in the eye of Paddy the Beaver a he reply : `` Well , now that you have find out that you ca n't do that , because I be big than you and can stop you , what be you go to do about it ? ''
`` I do n't know , '' say Jerry Muskrat sadly .
`` I do n't see what we can do about it .
Of course you be big and strong and can do just a you please , but it do n't seem right that we who have live here so long should have to move and go away from all that we love so just because you , a stranger , happen to want to live here .
I tell you what ! ''
Jerry 's eye sparkle a a brand new thought come to him .
`` Could n't you come down and live in the Smiling Pool with u ?
I 'm sure there be room enough ! ''
Paddy the Beaver shake his head .
`` No , '' say he , and Jerry 's heart sank .
`` No , I ca n't do that because down there there be n't any of the kind of food I eat .
Besides , I would n't feel at all safe in the Smiling Pool .
You see , I always live in the wood .
No , I could n't possibly come down to live in the Smiling Pool .
But I 'm truly sorry that I have make you so much worry , Cousin Jerry , and I 'm go to prove it to you .
Now you sit right here until I come back . ''
Before Jerry realize what he be go to do , Paddy the Beaver dive into the pond , and a he disappear , his broad tail hit the water such a slap that it make Jerry jump .
Then there begin a great disturbance down under water .
In a few minute up bob a stick , and then another and another , and the water grow so muddy that Jerry could n't see what be go on .
Paddy be go a long time .
Jerry wonder how he could stay under water so long without air .
All the time Paddy be just fool him .
He would come up to the surface , stick his nose out , nothing more , fill his lung with fresh air , and go down again .
Suddenly Jerry Muskrat hear a sound that make him prick up his funny little short ear and whirl about so that he could look over the other side of the dam into the Laughing Brook .
What do you think that sound be ?
Why , it be the sound of rush water , the sweet sound Jerry have listen to for a long time .
There be a great hole in the dam , and already the brook be begin to laugh a the water rush down it .
`` How do you like that , Cousin Jerry ? ''
say a voice right in his ear .
Paddy the Beaver have climb up beside him , and his eye be twinkle .
`` It -- it 's splendid ! ''
cry Jerry .
`` But -- but you 've spoil your dam ! ''
`` Oh , that 's all right , '' reply Paddy .
`` I do n't really want it now , anyway .
I do n't usually build dam at this time of year , and I build this one just for fun because it seem such a nice place to build one .
You see , I be travel through here , and it seem such a nice place , that I think I would stay a while .
I do n't know anything about the Smiling Pool , you know .
Now , I guess I 'll have to move on and find a place where I can make a pond in the fall that will not trouble other people .
You see , I do n't like to be trouble myself , and so I do n't want to trouble other people .
This Green Forest be a very nice place . ''
`` The very nice place in all the world except the Green Meadows and the Smiling Pool ! ''
reply Jerry promptly .
`` Wo n't you stay , Cousin Paddy ?
I 'm sure we would all like to have you . ''
`` Of course we would , '' say a gruff voice right beside them .
It be Grandfather Frog .
Paddy the Beaver look thoughtful .
`` Perhaps I will , '' say he , `` if I can find some good hiding-places in the Laughing Brook . ''
CHAPTER XXIV : A Merry Home-Going `` The Laughing Brook be merry And so be I , '' cry Jerry .
Grandfather Frog say he be too .
And Spotty be , the others know .
The tree stand with wet foot where just a little while before have be the strange pond in the Green Forest , the pond make by the dam of Paddy the Beaver .
In the dam be a great hole make by Paddy himself .
Through the Green Forest ring the laughter of the Laughing Brook , for once more the water run deep between it bank .
And in the heart of Grandfather Frog and Jerry Muskrat and Spotty the Turtle be laughter also , for now the Smiling Pool would smile once more , and they could go home in peace and happiness .
And there be one more who laugh .
Who be it ?
Why , Paddy the Beaver to be sure , and his be the best laugh of all , for it be because he have bring happiness to others .
`` You beat me up here to the dam , but you wo n't beat me back to the Smiling Pool , '' cry Jerry Muskrat to Spotty the Turtle .
Spotty laugh good-naturedly .
`` You 'd better not stop to eat or play or sleep on the way then , '' say he , `` for I shall keep right on go all the time .
I 've find that be the only way to get anywhere . ''
`` Let u all go down together '' say Grandfather Frog .
`` We can help each other over the bad place . ''
Jerry Muskrat laugh until he have to hold his side at the very thought of Grandfather Frog or Spotty the Turtle be able to help him , but he be very good-natured , and so he agree that they should all go down together .
Paddy the Beaver say that he would go , too , so off the four start , Jerry Muskrat and Paddy the Beaver swim side by side , and behind them Grandfather Frog and Spotty the Turtle .
Now Spotty the Turtle be a very slow traveler on land , but in the water Spotty be not so slow .
In fact , it be not long before Grandfather Frog find that he be the one who could not keep up .
You see , while he be a great diver and can swim fast for a short distance , he be soon tire out .
Pretty soon he be puff and blow and drop far and far behind .
By and by , Spotty the Turtle look back .
There be Grandfather Frog just tumble head first over a little waterfall .
He come up choking and gasping and kick his long legs very feebly .
Spotty climb out on a rock and wait .
He help Grandfather Frog out beside him , and when Grandfather Frog have once more gotten his breath , what do you think Spotty do ?
Why , he take Grandfather Frog right on his back and start on again .
Now Jerry Muskrat and Paddy the Beaver , be great swimmer , be soon out of sight .
All at once Jerry remember that they have agree to go back together , and down in his heart he felt a little bit mean when he look for Grandfather Frog and Spotty the Turtle and could see nothing of them .
So he and Paddy sit down to wait .
After what seem a long time , they saw something queer bob along in the water .
`` It 's Grandfather Frog , '' cry Paddy the Beaver .
`` No , it 's Spotty the Turtle , '' say Jerry Muskrat .
`` It 's both , '' reply Paddy , begin to laugh .
Just then Spotty tumble over another waterfall which he have n't see , and of course Grandfather Frog go with him and lose his hold on Spotty 's back .
`` I have an idea ! ''
cry Paddy .
`` What be it ? ''
ask Jerry .
`` Why , Grandfather Frog can ride on my flat tail , '' reply Paddy , `` and then we 'll go slow enough for Spotty to keep up with u . ''
And so it be that just a the first moonbeam kiss the Smiling Pool , out of the Laughing Brook swim the merry party that ever be see .
`` Chugarum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog .
`` It be good to be home , but I think I would travel often , if I could have the tail of Paddy the Beaver for a boat . ''
CHAPTER XXV : Paddy The Beaver Decides To Stay `` The fair Green Meadows spreading wide , The Smiling Pool and Laughing Brook -- They fill our heart with joy and pride ; We love their every hidden nook . ''
So say Jerry Muskrat , a he climb up on the Big Rock in the middle of the Smiling Pool , with Paddy the Beaver beside him , and watch the dear Smiling Pool dimpling and smiling in the moonlight , a he have so often see it before the great trouble have come .
`` Chugarum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog in his great deep voice from the bulrush .
`` One never know how great their blessing be until they have be lose and find again . ''
The bulrush nod , a if they too be think of this .
You see their foot be once more in the cool water .
Paddy the Beaver seem to understand just how every one felt , and he smile to himself a he saw how happy these new friend of his be .
`` It surely be a very nice place here , and I do n't wonder that you could n't bear to leave it , '' say he .
`` I 'm sorry that I make you all that trouble and worry , but you see I do n't know . ''
`` Oh , that 's all right , '' reply Jerry Muskrat , who be now very proud of his big cousin .
`` I hope that now you see how nice it be , you will stay and make your home here . ''
Paddy the Beaver look back at the great black shadow which he know be the Green Forest .
Way over in the middle of it he hear the hunting-call of Hooty the Owl .
Then he look out over the Green Meadows , and from way over on the far side of them sound the bark of Reddy Fox , and it be answer by the deep voice of Bowser the Hound up in Farmer Brown 's dooryard .
For some reason that last sound make Paddy the Beaver shiver a little , just a the voice of Hooty the Owl make the small people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows shiver when they hear it .
Paddy be n't afraid of Hooty or of Reddy Fox , but Bowser 's great voice be new to him , and somehow the very sound of it make him afraid .
You see , the Green Meadows be so strange and open that he do n't feel at all at home , for he dearly love the deep part of the Green Forest .
`` No , '' say Paddy the Beaver , `` I ca n't possibly live here in the Smiling Pool .
It be a very nice pool , but it would n't do at all for me , Cousin Jerry .
I would n't feel safe here a minute .
Besides , there be nothing to eat here . ''
`` Oh , yes , there be , '' Jerry Muskrat interrupt .
`` There be lily-roots and the nice fresh-water clam and -- '' `` But there be no tree , '' say Paddy the Beaver , `` and you know I have to have tree . ''
Jerry star at Paddy a if he do n't understand .
`` Do -- do you eat tree ? ''
he ask finally .
Paddy laugh .
`` Just the bark , '' say he , `` and I have to have a great deal of it . ''
Jerry look as disappointed a he felt .
`` Of course you ca n't stay then , '' say he , `` and -- and I have think that we would have such good time together . ''
Paddy 's eye twinkle .
`` Perhaps we may yet , '' say he .
`` You see I have about make up my mind that I will stay a while along the Laughing Brook in the Green Forest , and you can come to see me there .
On our way down I saw a very nice hole in the bank that I think will make me a good house for the present , and you can come up there to see me .
But if I do stay , you and Grandfather Frog and Spotty the Turtle must keep my secret .
No one must know that I be there .
Will you ? ''
`` Of course we will ! ''
cry Jerry Muskrat and Grandfather Frog and Spotty the Turtle together .
`` Then I 'll stay , '' say Paddy the Beaver , dive into the Smiling Pool with a great splash .
And so one of Jerry Muskrat 's great adventure end in the finding of his big cousin , Paddy the Beaver .

XI JIMMY SKUNK KEEPS HIS WORD Keep your word , whate'er you do , And to your inmost self be true .
When Jimmy Skunk shout down the hall of Johnny Chuck 's old house to Peter Rabbit that he would come back at dark , he be half joking .
He do it to make Peter uneasy and to worry him .
The truth be , Jimmy be no long angry at all .

Yes , Sir , I 'll have to go back .

XII JIMMY SKUNK AND UNC ' BILLY POSSUM MEET Jimmy Skunk amble along down the Lone Little Path through the Green Forest .

Jimmy never do hurry .

Now and then Jimmy stop to turn over a bit of bark or a stick , hop to find some fat beetle .
But it be plain to see that he have something besides fat beetle on his mind .
Up the Lone Little Path through the Green Forest shuffle Unc ' Billy Possum .

It be too warm to hurry .

And sometimes Unc ' Billy do worry .
You see , there be people who think that Unc ' Billy would make a very good dinner .
Unc ' Billy do n't think he would .

So occasionally , when he discover one of these people who think he would make a good dinner , he worry a little .
But just now Unc ' Billy be neither hurry nor worrying .
There be no need of do either , and Unc ' Billy never do anything that there be no need of do .
So Unc ' Billy shuffle up the Lone Little Path , and Jimmy Skunk amble down the Lone Little Path , and right at a bend in the Lone Little Path they meet .

XIV A LITTLE SOMETHING ABOUT EGGS `` An egg , '' say Jimmy Skunk , `` be good ; It 's very good indeed to eat . ''
`` An egg , '' say Mrs. Grouse , `` be dear ; ` Twill hatch into a baby sweet . ''
So in the matter of egg , a in a great many other matter , it all depend on the point of view .
To Jimmy Skunk and Unc ' Billy Possum egg be look on from the viewpoint of something to eat .
Their stomach prompt them to think of egg .
Eggs be good to fill empty stomach .
The mere thought of egg will make Jimmy and Unc ' Billy smack their lip .
They say they `` love '' egg , but they do n't .
They `` like '' them , which be quite different .
But Mrs. Grouse and most of the other feathered people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows and the Old Orchard really do `` love '' egg .
It be the heart instead of the stomach that respond to the thought of egg .
To them egg be almost as precious a baby , because they know that some day , some day very soon , those egg will become baby .
There be a few feathered folk , I be sorry to say , who `` love '' their own egg , but `` like '' the egg of other people -- like them just a Jimmy Skunk and Unc ' Billy Possum do , to eat .
Blacky the Crow be one and his cousin , Sammy Jay , be another .
So in the springtime there be always a great deal of matching of wit between the little people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows and the Old Orchard .
Those who have egg try to keep them a secret or to build the nest that hold them where none who like to eat them can get them ; and those who have an appetite for egg try to find them .
When Unc ' Billy Possum suddenly change the subject by ask Jimmy Skunk if he have find any nice fresh egg lately , he touch a subject very close to Jimmy 's heart .
I should have say , rather , his stomach .
To tell the truth , it be a longing for some egg that have bring Jimmy to the Green Forest .
He know that somewhere there Mrs. Grouse must be hide a nestful of the very nice of egg , and it be to hunt for these that he have come .
`` No , '' reply Jimmy , `` I have n't have any luck at all this spring .
I 've almost forget what an egg taste like .

Jimmy look very innocent a he ask this .

he demand .
`` Ah reckons Mrs. Grouse have n't get any mo ' aiggs than Ah could comfortably take care of mahself , not to mention Mrs. Possum . ''
Here Unc ' Billy look back over his shoulder to make sure that old Mrs. Possum be n't within hearing , and Jimmy Skunk chuckle .
`` Seems to me , Brer Skunk , yo ' might well do your aigg hunt on the Green Meadows and leave the Green Forest to me , '' continue Unc ' Billy .
`` That would be no mo ' than fair .
Yo ' know Ah never do hanker fo ' to get far away from tree , but yo ' do n't mind .
Besides there be mo ' aiggs for yo ' to find on the Green Meadows than there be fo ' me to find in the Green Forest .
A right smart lot of bird make their nest on the ground there .
There be Brer Bob White and Brer Meadowlark and Brer Bobolink and Brer Field Sparrow and Brer -- '' `` Never mind any more , Unc ' Billy , '' interrupt Jimmy Skunk .
`` I know all about them .

XV A SECOND MEETING Jimmy Skunk could n't think of anything but egg .

-LSB- Illustration -RSB- XVI A MATTER OF POLITENESS It cost not much to be polite And , furthermore , it 's always right .

Unc ' Billy want Jimmy to go first because he always feel safer behind Jimmy than in front of him .
He have great respect for that little bag of scent that Jimmy carry , and he know that when Jimmy make use of it , he always throw it in front and never behind him .
Jimmy seldom use it , but sometimes he do if he happen to be startle and think danger near .

It be n't politeness at all on the part of Unc ' Billy .

Each be think of self .

But something do happen .

CHAPTER I PETER RABBIT MEETS LIGHTFOOT Peter Rabbit be on his way back from the pond of Paddy the Beaver deep in the Green Forest .
He have just see Mr. and Mrs. Quack start toward the Big River for a brief visit before leave on their long , difficult journey to the far-away Southland .
Farewells be always rather sad , and this particular farewell have leave Peter with a lump in his throat , -- a queer , choky feeling .
`` If I be sure that they would return next spring , it would n't be so bad , '' he mutter .
`` It 's those terrible gun .
I know what it be to have to watch out for them .
Farmer Brown 's boy use to hunt me with one of them , but he do n't any more .
But even when he do hunt me it be n't anything like what the Ducks have to go through .
If I keep my eye and ear open , I could tell when a hunter be come and could hide in a hole if I want to .
I never have to worry about my meal .
But with the Ducks it be a thousand time worse .
They 've get to eat while make that long journey , and they can eat only where there be the right kind of food .
Hunters with terrible gun know where those place be and hide there until the Ducks come , and the Ducks have no way of know whether the hunter be wait for them or not .
That be n't hunt .
It 's -- it 's -- '' `` Well , what be it ?
What be you talk to yourself about , Peter Rabbit ? ''
Peter look up with a start to find the soft , beautiful eye of Lightfoot the Deer gaze down at him over the top of a little hemlock tree .
`` It 's awful , '' declare Peter .
`` It 's bad than unfair .
It do n't give them any chance at all . ''
`` I suppose it must be so if you say so , '' reply Lightfoot , `` but you might tell me what all this awfulness be about . ''
Peter grin .
Then he begin at the beginning and tell Lightfoot all about Mr. and Mrs. Quack and the many danger they must face on their long journey to the far-away Southland and back again in the spring , all because of the heartless hunter with terrible gun .
Lightfoot listen and his great soft eye be fill with pity for the Quack family .
`` I hope they will get through all right , '' say he , `` and I hope they will get back in the spring .
It be bad enough to be hunt by men at one time of the year , a no one know good than I do , but to be hunt in the spring as well a in the fall be more than twice a bad .
Men be strange creature .
I do not understand them at all .
None of the people of the Green Forest would think of do such terrible thing .
I suppose it be quite right to hunt others in order to get enough to eat , though I be thankful to say that I never have have to do that , but to hunt others just for the fun of hunting be something I can not understand at all .
And yet that be what men seem to do it for .
I guess the trouble be they never have be hunt themselves and do n't know how it feel .
Sometimes I think I 'll hunt one some day just to teach him a lesson .
What be you laugh at , Peter ? ''
`` At the idea of you hunt a man , '' reply Peter .
`` Your heart be all right , Lightfoot , but you be too timid and gentle to frighten any one .

His eye , which Peter have always think so soft and gentle , seem to flash fire .
`` Oh ! ''
cry Peter in a faint , frightened-sounding voice and leap to one side before it enter his foolish little head that Lightfoot be just pretend .

`` Did you say I could n't frighten any one ? ''
he demand .
`` I -- I do n't know you could look so terribly fierce , '' stammer Peter .
`` Those antler look really dangerous when you point them that way .
Why -- why -- what be that hang to them ?
It look like bit of old fur .
Have you be tear somebody 's coat , Lightfoot ? ''
Peter 's eye be wide with wonder and suspicion .

And if those be new one , where be the old one ?
Show me the old one , and perhaps I 'll believe that these be new one .
The idea of try to make me believe that antler grow just like plant !
I 've see Bossy the Cow all summer and I know she have get the same horn she have last summer .
New antler indeed ! ''
`` You be quite right , Peter , quite right about Bossy the Cow .
She never have new horn , but that be n't any reason why I should n't have new antler , be it ? ''
replied Lightfoot patiently .
`` Her horn be quite different from my antler .
I have a new pair every year .
You have n't see me all summer , have you , Peter ? ''
`` No , I do n't remember that I have , '' reply Peter , try very hard to remember when he have last see Lightfoot .
`` I know you have n't , '' retort Lightfoot .
`` I know it because I have be hide in a place you never visit . ''
`` What have you be hide for ? ''
demand Peter .
`` For my new antler to grow , '' reply Lightfoot .
`` When my new antler be grow , I want to be away by myself .
I do n't like to be see without them or with half grown one .
Besides , I be very uncomfortable while the new antler be grow and I want to be alone . ''
Lightfoot speak a if he really mean every word he say , but still Peter could n't , he just could n't believe that those wonderful great antler have grow out of Lightfoot 's head in a single summer .
`` Where do you leave your old one and when do they come off ? ''
he ask , and there be doubt in the very tone of his voice .
`` They drop off last spring , but I do n't remember just where , '' reply Lightfoot .
`` I be too glad to be rid of them to notice where they drop .
You see they be loose and uncomfortable , and I have n't any more use for them because I know that my new one would be big and well .
I 've get one more point on each than I have last year . ''
Lightfoot begin once more to rub his antler against the tree to get off the queer rag hang to them and to polish the point .
Peter watch in silence for a few minute .
Then , all his suspicion return , he say : `` But you have n't tell me anything about those rag hang to your antler . ''
`` And you have n't believe what I have already tell you , '' retort Lightfoot .
`` I do n't like tell thing to people who wo n't believe me . ''
CHAPTER III LIGHTFOOT TELLS HOW HIS ANTLERS GREW It be hard to believe what seem impossible .
And yet what seem impossible to you may be a very commonplace matter to some one else .
So it do not do to say that a thing can not be possible just because you can not understand how it can be .
Peter Rabbit want to believe what Lightfoot the Deer have just tell him , but somehow he could n't .
If he have see those antler grow , it would have be another matter .
But he have n't see Lightfoot since the very last of winter , and then Lightfoot have wear just such handsome antler a he now have .
So Peter really could n't be blame for not be able to believe that those old one have be lose and in their place new one have grow in just the few month of spring and summer .
But Peter do n't blame Lightfoot in the least , because he have tell Peter that he do n't like to tell thing to people who would n't believe what he tell them when Peter have ask him about the rag hang to his antler .
`` I 'm try to believe it , '' he say , quite humbly .
`` It 's all true , '' break in another voice .
Peter jump and turn to find his big cousin , Jumper the Hare .
Unseen and unheard , he have steal up and have overhear what Peter and Lightfoot have say .
`` How do you know it be true ? ''
snap Peter a little crossly , for Jumper have startle him .
`` Because I saw Lightfoot 's old antler after they have fall off , and I often saw Lightfoot while his new one be grow , '' retort Jumper .
`` All right !
I 'll believe anything that Lightfoot tell me if you say it be true , '' declare Peter , who greatly admire his cousin , Jumper .
`` Now tell me about those rag , Lightfoot .
Please do . ''
Lightfoot could n't resist that `` please . ''
`` Those rag be what be leave of a kind of cover which protect the antler while they be grow , a I tell you before , '' say he .
`` Very soon after my old one drop off the new one begin to grow .
They be not hard , not at all like they be now .
They be soft and very tender , and the blood run through them just a it do through our body .
They be cover with a sort of skin with hair on it like thin fur .
The end be not sharply point a they now be , but be big and round , like knob .
They be not like antler at all , and they make my head hot and be very uncomfortable .
That be why I hide away .
They grow very fast , so fast that every day I could see by look at my reflection in water that they be a little long .
It seem to me sometimes a if all my strength go into those new antler .
And I have to be very careful not to hit them against anything .
In the first place it would have hurt , and in the second place it might have spoil the shape of them .
`` When they have grow to the length you now see , they begin to shrink and grow hard .
The knob on the end shrink until they become point .
As soon a they stop grow the blood stop flow up in them , and a they become hard they be no long tender .
The skin which have cover them grow dry and split , and I rub it off on tree and bush .
The little rag you see be what be leave , but I will soon be rid of those .
Then I shall be ready to fight if need be and will fear no one save man , and will fear him only when he have a terrible gun with him . ''
Lightfoot toss his head proudly and rattle his wonderful antler against the near tree .
`` Is n't he handsome , '' whisper Peter to Jumper the Hare ; `` and do you ever hear of anything so wonderful a the growing of those new antler in such a short time ?
It be hard to believe , but I suppose it must be true . ''
`` It be , '' reply Jumper , `` and I tell you , Peter , I would hate to have Lightfoot try those antler on me , even though I be big a a man .
You 've always think of Lightfoot a timid and afraid , but you should see him when he be angry .
Few people care to face him then . ''
CHAPTER IV THE SPIRIT OF FEAR When the day grow cold and the night be clear , There stalk abroad the spirit of fear .
Lightfoot the Deer .
It be sad but true .
Autumn be often call the sad time of the year , and it be the sad time .
But it should n't be .
Old Mother Nature never intend that it should be .
She mean it to be the glad time .
It be the time when all the little people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows have get over the care and worry of bring up family and teach their child how to look out for themselves .
It be the season when food be plentiful , and every one be fat and be , or ought to be , care free .
It be the season when Old Mother Nature intend all her little people to be happy , to have nothing to worry them for the little time before the come of cold weather and the hard time which cold weather always bring .
But instead of this , a grim , dark figure go stalk over the Green Meadows and through the Green Forest , and it be call the Spirit of Fear .
It peer into every hiding-place and wherever it find one of the little people it send little cold chill over him , little chill which jolly , round , bright Mr. Sun can not chase away , though he shine his bright .
All night as well a all day the Spirit of Fear search out the little people of the Green Meadows and the Green Forest .
It will not let them sleep .
It will not let them eat in peace .
It drive them to seek new hiding-places and then drive them out of those .
It keep them ever ready to fly or run at the slight sound .
Peter Rabbit be think of this a he sit at the edge of the dear Old Briar-patch , look over to the Green Forest .
The Green Forest be no longer just green ; it be of many color , for Old Mother Nature have set Jack Frost to paint the leaf of the maple-trees and the beech-trees , and the birch-trees and the poplar-trees and the chestnut-trees , and he have do his work well .
Very , very lovely be the red and yellow and brown against the dark green of the pine and the spruce and the hemlock .
The Purple Hills be more softly purple than at any other season of the year .
It be all very , very beautiful .
But Peter have no thought for the beauty of it all , for the Spirit of Fear have visit even the dear Old Briar-patch , and Peter be afraid .
It be n't fear of Reddy Fox , or Redtail the Hawk , or Hooty the Owl , or Old Man Coyote .
They be forever try to catch him , but they do not strike terror to his heart because he felt quite smart enough to keep out of their clutch .
To be sure , they give him sudden fright sometimes , when they happen to surprise him , but these fright last only until he reach the near bramble-tangle or hollow log where they could not get at him .
But the fear that chill his heart now never leave him even for a moment .
And Peter know that this same fear be clutch at the heart of Bob White , hiding in the brown stubble ; of Mrs. Grouse , squat in the thick bramble-tangle in the Green Forest ; of Uncle Billy Possum and Bobby Coon in their hollow tree ; of Jerry Muskrat in the Smiling Pool ; of Happy Jack Squirrel , hide in the tree top ; of Lightfoot the Deer , lie in the closest thicket he could find .
It be even clutch at the heart of Granny and Reddy Fox and of great , big Buster Bear .
It seem to Peter that no one be so big or so small that this terrible Spirit of Fear have not search him out .
Far in the distance sound a sudden bang .
Peter jump and shiver .
He know that every one else who have hear that bang have jump and shiver just a he have .
It be the season of hunter with terrible gun .
It be man who have send this terrible Spirit of Fear to chill the heart of the little meadow and forest people at this very time when Old Mother Nature have make all thing so beautiful and have intend that they should be happiest and most free from care and worry .
It be man who have make the autumn a sad time instead of a glad time , the very sad time of all the year , when Old Mother Nature have do her best to make it the most beautiful .
`` I do n't understand these men creature , '' say Peter to little Mrs. Peter , a they star fearfully out from the dear Old Briar-patch .
`` They seem to find pleasure , actually find pleasure , in try to kill u .
I do n't understand them at all .
They have n't any heart .
That must be the reason ; they have n't any heart . ''
